I answered that question correctly.	Nàge wèntí wǒ huídáduì le.	那个问题我回答对了。
We can all understand the teacher's Chinese.	Lǎoshī shuō de zhōngwén, wǒmen doū néng tīngdǒng.	老师说的中文，我们都能听懂。
He hasn't finished reading.	Tā méi kànwán.	他没看完。
Has he finished reading?	Tā kànwánle méiyǒu?	他看完了没有？
Yesterday's meeting was very helpful to me.	Zuótiān de huìyì duì wǒ yǒu hěn dà de bāngzhu.	昨天的会议对我有很大的帮助。
He said to me: "Who are you?"	Tā duì wǒ shuō: "Nǐ shi shéi?"	他对我说：＂你是谁？＂
Although we've only been studying for a short time, we've already learned a lot.	Suīrán wǒmen xuéxí de shíjiān hěn duǎn, dànshi yǐjīng xuéle bù shǎo dōngxi le.	虽然我们学习的时间很短，但是已经学了不少东西了。
Although this text is long, it's not too hard.	Zhè kè kèwèn suīrán hěn cháng, dànshi bú tài nán.	这课课文虽然很长，但是不太难。
His Chinese still has some grammar mistakes.	Tā shuōde zhōngwén hái yǒu yìxiē yǔfǎ cuòwu.	他说的中文还有一些语法错误。

I'm not done reading.	Wǒ méi kànwán.	我没看完。
I heard him upstairs reading the text out loud.	Wǒ tīngjian tā zài lóushang dàshēng de niàn kèwén.	我听见他在楼上大声地念课文。
If you go to the bookstore, buy me a grammar.	Nǐ yàoshi qù shūdiàn, jiù gěi wǒ mǎi yìběn yǔfǎ.	你要是去书店，就给我买一本语法。
If there's time, I'll go visit you.	Yàoshi yǒu shíjian, wǒ jiù qù zhǎo nǐ.	要是有时间，我就去找你。
Explain it to me once more.	Nǐ zài gěi wǒ jiǎng yíbiàn ba.	你再给我讲一遍吧。
He explained it once again.	Tā yòu jiǎngle yíbiàn.	他又讲了一遍。
I'd like to see it again.	Wǒ xiǎng zài kàn yíbiàn.	我想再看一遍。
I read it (just) five times and then read it fluently.	Wǒ niànle wǔbiàn jiù niànshú le.	我念了五遍就念熟了。
Only (after) reading it five times did I read it skillfully.	Wǒ niànle wǔbiàn cái niànshú.	我念了五遍才念熟。
As soon as he reviewed them, he had them memorized.	Tā fùxíle jiù jìzhù le.	他复习了就记住了。
It was only on reviewing them that he had them memorized.	Tā fùxíle cái jìzhù.	他复习了才记住。
I saw him walking in front.	Wǒ kànjian tā zài qiánbian zǒu.	我看见他在前边走。
He didn't hear.	Tā méi tīngjian.	他没听见。
I answered wrong.	Wǒ huídá cuò le.	我回答错了。
You still need to practice again.	Nǐ hái yào zài lìanxí.	你还要再练习。
To memorize Chinese characters you need to practice a lot.	Jì hànzì yào duō liànxí.	记汉字要多练习。
The especially hard ones you definitely have to write more times.	Tèbié nán de yídìng yào duō xiě jǐbiàn.	特别难的一定要多写几遍。
If you write them too few times, it's easy to forget.	Yàoshi xiěde tài shǎo, jiù róngyi wàng.	要是写得太少，就容易忘。
Finally he said: "You yourself need to be hardworking."	Zuìhòu tā shuō: "bìxū zìjǐ nǔlì."	最后他说：＂必须自己努力＂。

I looked, but I didn't see it.	Wǒ kàn, dànshi méi kànjian.	我看，但是没看见。

He told me to read it again; I read it again.	Tā jiào wǒ zài niàn yíbiàn, wǒ jiù yòu niànle yíbiàn.	他叫我再念一遍，我就又念了一遍。
He came yesterday, he came again today, tomorrow he wants to come yet again.	Tā zuótiān lái le, jīntiān yòu lái le, míngtiān hái yào zài lái.	他昨天来了，今天又来了，明天还要再来。

The weather's gotten warmer, we can study outside again.	Tiānqì nuǎnhuo le, wǒmen yòu kěyǐ zài wàibian xuéxí le.	天气暖和了，我们又可以在外边学习了。
He got there by six, I only arrived at nine.	Tā lìudiǎn jiù lái le, wǒ jiǔdiǎn cái lái.	他六点就来了，我九点才来。

I study till 10:30 every night.	Měitiān wǎnshang wǒ dōu xuéxídào shídiǎnbàn.	每天晚上我都学习到十点半。

He explained it to me again a bit.	Tā yòu gěi wǒ jiǎnglejiang.	他又给我讲了讲。

He also (moreover) referred to the fact that Chinese students often go to communes to take part in physical work.	Tā hái tándào zhōngguó xuéshēng chángcháng dào rénmín gōngshè qù cānjiā láodòng.	他还谈到中国学生常常到人民公社去参加劳动。

How's the writing in this book?	Zhè běn shū xǐe de zěnme yàng?	这本书写得怎么样？
How can it be that he isn't coming back even now?	Tā zěnme xiànzài hái bù huílái?	他怎么现在还不回来？
He just came to the school on Sunday.	Tā shi xīngqīrì gāng lái xuéxiaò de.	他是星期日刚来学校的。
I'm just back from seeing my friend off.	Wǒ gāng qù sòng péngyou húilái.	我刚去送朋友回来。
Just as soon as they visited the factory they went to see the movie.	Tāmen gāng cānguānle gōngchǎng, yòu qù kàn diànyǐng le.	他们刚参观了工厂，又去看电影了。
I was originally thinking to go to the movie, but then he came to visit me.	Wǒ běnlái xiǎng qù kàn diànyǐng, hòulái tā lái zhǎo wǒ.	我本来想去看电影，后来他来找我。
We two didn't know each other before; it was only coming to this school that we met.	Wǒmen liǎngge rén běnlài bú rènshi, lái zhège xuéxiaò yǐhòu cái rènshi de.	我们两个人本来不认识，来这个学校以后才认识的。
We used to have two classes in the afternoon, now we have just one.	Xìawǔ běnlái yǒu liǎngjié kè, xiànzài zhǐ yǒu yì jié kè le.	下午本来有两节课，现在只有一节课了。
I was thinking to go to the park, but then I thought I'd better read, so finally I just read.	Wǒ xiǎng qù gōngyuán, yòu xiǎng yīnggāi kànshū, hòulái jiù kànle shū.	我想去公园，又想应该看书，后来就看了书。
I'm thinking to go give him the book, but I'm afraid he's not home.	Wǒ xiǎng gěi tā sòng shū qù, yòu pà tā bú zài jiā.	我想给他送书去，又怕他不在家。
Walk south from here and you'll get to that factory.	Cóng zhèr xiàng nán zǒu, jiù dào nàge gōngchǎng le.	从这儿向南走，就到那个工厂了。
We should learn from him.	Wǒmen yīnggāi xiàng tā xuéxí.	我们应该向他学习。
I introduced my friend to a lot of well-known places.	Wǒ xiàng wǒ péngyou jièshàole hěn duō yǒumíng de dìfang.	我向我朋友介绍了很多有名的地方。
I went to the station to meet a friend.	Wǒ dào chēzhàn qù jiē yíge péngyou.	我到车站去接一个朋友。
He just came to Peking from our country.	Tā gāng cóng wǒmen guójiā lái běijīng.	他刚从我们国家来北京。
Originally I thought I'd ride my bike to the station.	Wǒ běnlái xiǎng qí zìxíngchē qù chēzhàn.	我本来想骑自行车去车站。
I decided to go by car.	Wǒ juédìng zuò qìchē qù.	我决定坐汽车去。
I don't speak Chinese, didn't you know?	Wǒ bú huì zhōngwén, nǐ búshì zhīdao ma?	我不会中文，你不是知道吗？
I laughed/smiled.	Wǒ xiàole.	我笑了。
I'm already used to it.	Wǒ yǐjīng xíguàn le.	我已经习惯了。
We passed through TianAnMen square.	Wǒmen jīngguò le tiānānmén guǎngchǎng.	我们经过了天安门广场。
That's the people's heroes commemorative monument.	Nà shi rénmín yīngxióng jìniànbēi.	那是人民英雄纪念碑。
When you have time, come here and have a look.	Nǐ yǒu shíjiān, lái zhèr kànkan ba.	你有时间，来这儿看看吧。
I said, furthermore: "You ought to study more."	Wǒ bìngqiě shuō: Nǐ yīnggāi duō xuéxí.	我并且说：你应该多学习。
Just as soon as he went out it started raining.	Tā gāng chūqù, jiù xià yǔ le.	他刚出去，就下雨了。
You've learned how to use a dictionary.	Nǐ xuéhuìle chá zìdiǎn.	你学会了查字典。
He just went out; why did he come back?	Tā gāng chūqu, wèishénme yòu huíláile?	他刚出去，为什么又回来了？
I'm thinking to go out, on the other hand I'm afraid it'll rain.	Wǒ xiǎng chūqù, yòu pà xiàyǔ.	我想出去，又怕下雨。
I'm in class. (4 ways)	Wǒ zhèngzài shàngkè | Wǒ zhèng shàngkè | Wǒ zài shàngkè | Wǒ shàngkè ne.	我正在上课｜我正上课｜我在上课｜我上课呢。
I'm right in the middle of translating a sentence.	Wǒ zhèngzài fānyi jùzi ne.	我正在翻译句子呢。
He's exercising (at the moment).	Tā zài duànliàn shēntǐ.	他在锻炼身体。
When I went in she was telling the children a story.	Wǒ jìnqu de shíhou, tā zhèng gěi háizimen jiǎng gùshi ne.	我进去的时候，她正给孩子们讲故事呢。
I was looking for him and in he came.	Wǒ zhèng zhǎo tā, tā jìnlai le.	我正找他，他进来了。
Are you doing the exercises?  No, I'm reading the text.	Nǐ zài zuò liànxí ma?  Méiyǒu, wǒ niàn kèwén ne.	你在作练习吗？没有，我念课文呢。
I'm not writing characters, I'm reading a book.	Wǒ méi xiě hànzì, wǒ zhèng kàn shū ne.	我没写汉字，我正看书呢。
It's about to snow. (4 ways)	Yào xià xuě le | Jiùyaò xià xuě le | Kuài xià xuě le | Kuàiyaò xià xuě le.	要下雪了｜就要下雪了｜快下雪了｜快要下雪了。
He's going to get going right after 3.	Tā sāndiǎnzhōng jiùyào zǒu le.	他三点钟就要走了。
Are you just about done studying this textbook.	Zhèběn kèběn nǐ kuài xuéwán le ma?	这本课本你快学完了吗？
National Day is coming up.	Guóqìngjié kuàiyào dào le.	国庆节快要到了。
One day I went to visit him there.	Yǒu yì tiān, wǒ qù tā nàr.	有一天，我去他那儿。
It looks good, how's the sound?	Yàngzi hěn hǎokàn, shēngyin zěnme yàng?	样子很好看，声音怎么样？
Listen, now they're broadcasting Chinese music.	Nǐ tīng, xiànzài zhèng guǎngbō zhōngguó yīnyuè ne.	你听，现在正广播中国音乐呢。
He turned on the radio.	Tā kāikai shōuyīnjī.	他开开收音机。
Beijing is far.	Běijīng hěn yuǎn.	北京很远。
In a minute they're going to broadcast the news.	Yì huǐr jiù yào guǎngbō xīnwén le.	一会儿就要广播新闻了。
Can you understand the news program?	Xīnwén jiémù, nǐ néng tīngdǒng ma?	新闻节目，你能听懂吗？
I haven't got a lot of vocabulary yet.	Wǒ zhǎngwò de cí hái bù duō.	我掌握的词还不多。
I asked him what other programs are broadcast.	Wǒ wèn tā, hái guǎngbō yìxiē shénme jiémù.	我问他，还广播一些什么节目。
They also broadcast some simple short stories.	Hái guǎngbō yìxiē jiǎndān de xiǎo gùshi.	还广播一些简单的小故事。
They're broadcast for kids.	Shi duì háizimen guǎngbō de.	是对孩子们广播的。
The content is simple (unsophisticated).	Nèiróng hěn qiǎn.	内容很浅。
The sentences are not too complicated.	Jùzi bú tài fùzá.	句子不太复杂。
I can mostly understand (what I hear). 	Wǒ néng tīngdǒng dàgài de yìsi.	我能听懂大概的意思。
Just then we heard the news program start.	Zhè shíhou wǒmen tīngjian xīnwén jiémù kāishǐ le.	这时候我们听见新闻节目开始了。
He turns off the radio.	Tā guānshang shōuyīnjī.	他关上收音机。
He explained to me the advantages of listening to broadcasts for studying Chinese.	Tā gěi wǒ jiǎnglejiang tīng guǎngbō duì xué zhōngwén de hǎochu.	他给我讲了讲听广播对学中文的好处。
I feel very happy.	Wǒ juéde hěn gāoxìng.	我觉得很高兴。
It's raining.	Xià yǔ ne.	下雨呢。
I'm not reading a magazine, I'm reading a newspaper.	Wǒ méi kàn zázhì, wǒ kàn bào ne.	我没看杂志，我看报呢。

I first reviewed the text twice.	Wǒ xiān fùxíle liǎngbiàn kèwén.	我先复习了两遍课文。

In your letter you say that China's people highly prize the friendship between the people of our two countries.	Nǐ xìnli shuō, zhōngguó rénmín fēicháng zhēnshì wǒmen liǎngguó rénmín de yǒuyì.	你信里说，中国人民非常珍视我们两国人民的友谊。

There's a commune I once visited five years ago.	Yǒu yìge gōngshè, wǒ wǔnián qián cānguānguo yícì.	有一个公社，我五年前参观过一次。
The standard of living of commune members had risen (in some respects).	Shèyuán shēnghuó yǒule tígāo.	社员生活有了提高。
I saw that their production had some new developments.	Wǒ kàndào tāmen de shēngchǎn yǒule xīn de fāzhǎn.	我看到他们的生产有了新的发展。

His name is written on that dictionary.	Nàběn zìdiǎnshang xiězhe tā de míngzi.	那本字典上写着他的名字。

Smiling he greeted us.	Tā xiàozhe gēn wǒmen dǎ zhāohu.	他笑着跟我们打招呼。
They're walking (i.e. not driving).	Tāmen shi zǒuzhe qùde.	他们是走着去的。
The teacher asked us to tell stories while looking at pictures.	Lǎoshī ràng wǒmen kànzhe huàr jiǎng gùshi.	老师让我们看着画儿讲故事。
There are 40 or 50 books (set) on the shelf.	Shūjiàshang fàngzhe sìwǔshiběn shū.	书架上放着四五十本书。
There are 500 odd people sitting in the auditorium.	Lǐtángli zuòzhe wǔbǎiduō rén.	礼堂坐着五百多人。
Three of our classmates have left.	Wǒmen bān zǒule sānge tóngxué.	我们班走了三个同学。
I haven't finished writing it, I'll go on with it this afternoon.	Wǒ hái méi xiěwán, xiàwǔ jiēzhe xiě.	我还没写完，下午接着写。
He finished speaking and we proceeded to discuss it for a while.	Tā jiǎngwánle, jiēzhe wǒmen tǎolùnle yìhuǐr.	他讲完了，接着我们讨论了一会儿。
I want a thicker one.	Wǒ yào yíge hòu yídiǎnr de.	我要一个厚一点儿的。
I have a friend who got sick and is in the hospital.	Wǒ yǒu yíge péngyou bìngle, zhù zài yīyuànli.	我有一个朋友病了，住在医院里。
When I found his ward I knocked on the door and went in.	Zhǎodàole tāde bìngfáng, jiù qiāo mén jìnqu le.	找到了他的病房，就敲门进去了。
Don't get up.	Bú yào qǐlai le.	不要起来了。
He was lying down reading a book.	Tā zhèng tǎngzhe kàn shū ne.	他正躺着看书呢。
He made to get up.	Tā xiǎng yào qǐlai.	他想要起来。
It was very clean in the room.	Wūzili hěn gānjing.	屋子里很干净。
A table was placed next to the bed.	Chuáng pángbiān fàngzhe yìzhāng zhuōzi.	床旁边放着一张桌子。
The windows were all open.	Chuānghu dōu kāizhe.	窗户都开着。
The air was good.	Kōngqì hěn hǎo.	空气很好。
How's your health?	Nǐ shēntǐ qíngkuàng zěnme yàng?	你身体情况怎么样？
I take medicine and get injections every day.	Wǒ měitiān chī yào, dǎ zhēn.	我每天吃药，打针。
Are you used to life in the hospital?	Nǐ zài yīyuànli shēnghuó xíguàn bu xíguàn?	你在医院里生活习惯不习惯？
He's very concerned about me (i.e. caring).	Tā duì wǒ hěn guānxīn.	他对我很关心。
He makes me Chinese food.	Tā gěi wǒ zuò zhōngguó fàncài.	他给我做中国饭菜。
The doctor comes to attend him.	Dàifu lái gěi tā kànbìng.	大夫来给他看病。
I greatly appreciate your attention.	Wǒ fēicháng gǎnxiè nǐ duì wǒ de guānxīn.	我非常感谢你对我的关心。
I hope our two countries' peoples will forever mutally support each other.	Xīwàng wǒmen liǎngguó rénmín yǒngyuǎn hùxiāng zhīchí.	希望我们两国人民永远互相支持。
We chatted till after four.	Wǒmen tándào sìdiǎnduō zhōng.	我们谈到四点多钟。
I hope you get out quick (from the hospital).	Xīwàng nǐ zǎo diǎnr chūyuàn.	希望你早点儿出院。
No need to come see me again.	Búyòng zài lái kàn wǒ le.	不用再来看我了。
The windows are all (currently) open.	Chuānghu dōu kāizhe.	窗户都开着。
He's lying in bed (both progressive and continuous).	Tā zhèngzài chuángshang tǎngzhe ne.	他正在床上躺着呢。
We were right in the middle of talking when we heard someone outside listening.	Wǒmen zhèng shuōzhe huà, tīngjian wàibian yǒu rén tīng wǒmen.	我们正说着话，听见外边有人听我们。
He went out riding a bike.	Tā qízhe zìxíngchē chūqule.	他骑着自行车出去了。
The content of this text continues from the last one.	Zhè kè kèwén de nèiróng shi jiēzhe shàng yíkè de.	这课课文的内容是接着上一课的。
Tomorrow we'll continue along (explaining the lesson).	Míngtiān zài jiēzhe jiǎng.	明天再接着讲。
First the wind blew and then right away it started to rain.	Xiān guāfēng, jiēzhe jiù xià yǔ le.	先刮风，接着就下雨了。
Is there a map that's a bit bigger?	Dìtú yǒu dà diǎnr de ma?	地图有大点儿的吗？
Hope you get better soon.	Xīwàng nǐ kuài diǎnr hǎo.	希望你快点儿好。
He was going to China, and a lot of friends went to the station to see him off.	Tā yào qù zhōngguó le, hǎo xiē péngyou dào chēzhàn qù sòng tā.	他要去中国了，好些朋友到车站去送他。
He brought quite a few books.	Tā dàilái le hǎo duō shū.	他带来了好多书。
It's been a long time (since we met).	Wǒmen hǎo cháng shíjiān méi jiàn le.	我们好长时间没见了。
Let's go together to work out (you guys and me).	Zánmen yìqǐ qù duànliàn ba.	咱们一起去锻炼吧。
It's been quite a few days since we worked out.	Hǎo jǐ tiān méi duànliàn shēntǐ le.	好几天没锻炼身体了。
He can even read Chinese newspapers now.	Tā xiànzài lián zhōngwén bào dōu néng kàn le.	他现在连中文报都能看了。
Even I understood that story.	Nà ge gùshi lián wǒ dōu tīngdǒng le.	那个故事连我都听懂了。
He was in China for a short time and didn't even get to Shanghai.	Tā zài zhōngguó shíjiān hěn duǎn, lián shànghǎi yě méi qù.	他在中国时间很短，连上海也没去。
He translated it without even using a dictionary.	Tā lián zìdiǎn yě méi chá jiù fānyihǎo le.	他连字典也没查就翻译好了。
He didn't even see it, how could he know if it's good?	Tā lián kàn yě méi kàn, zěnme zhīdao hǎo bu hǎo ne?	他连看也没看，怎么知道好不好呢？
It's just seven o'clock now.	Xiànzài gāng qīdiǎn zhōng.	现在刚七点钟。
The post office isn't open yet.	Yóujú hái méi kāi mén ne.	邮局还没开门呢。
They're not back yet.	Tāmen hái méi huílai ne.	他们还没回来呢。
It's not too cold yet.	Hái bú tài lěng ne.	还不太冷呢。
It's okay not wear a coat.	Kěyi bù chuān dàyī.	可以不穿大衣。
They still can't even speak simple Chinese.	Lián jiǎndān de huà hái bú huì shuō ne.	连简单的话还不会说呢。
It doesn't matter, thin ones are okay.	Méi guānxi, báo de yě kěyǐ.	没关系，薄的也可以。
It's okay if we don't go this time.	Zhè cì bú qù méi guānxi.	这次不去没关系。
There'll be another chance (e.g. to go) later.	Yǐhòu hái huì yǒu jīhuì.	以后还会有机会。
A north wind was blowing and Lenin was still wearing an old coat.	Guāzhe běifēng, lièníng hái chuānzhe yíjiàn jiù dàyī.	刮着北风，列宁还穿着一件旧大衣。
He'd worn this coat for a good many years.	Zhè jiàn dàyī chuānle hǎo xiē nián le.	这件大衣穿了好些年了。
It was already patched in a good many places.	Hǎo jǐge dìfang yǐjīng bǔguo le.	好几个地方已经补过了。
They were afraid he'd freeze.	Tāmen pà tā dònghuài.	他们怕他冻坏。
They advised him to exchange (his coat) for a new one.	Tāmen quàn tā huàn yíjiàn xīn de.	他们劝他换一件新的。
Isn't everyone just as cold (as I am)?	Dàjiā búshì yíyàng lěng ma?	大家不是一样冷吗？
The revolution succeeded.	Gémìng shènglì le.	革命胜利了。
He's joking.	Tā kāi wánxiào.	他开玩笑。
His coat could be put in a museum.	Tā de dàyī kěyi jìn bówùguǎn le.	他的大衣可以进博物馆了。
Please immediately change to a new coat.	Qǐng mǎshàng huàn jiàn xīn dàyī ba.	情马上换件新大衣吧。
Otherwise, you might freeze.	Bùrán, nǐ huì dònghuài de.	不然你会冻坏的。
Holding him tightly by the hand, he said thanks.	Jǐn wòzhe tā de shǒu tā shuō xièxie.	紧喔着他的手他说谢谢。
Now that the revolution has succeeded, you think we (you and I) should dress a little better.	Nǐ yǐwéi gémìng shènglìle, zánmen jiù yīnggāi chuān de hǎo yìdiǎnr.	你以为革命胜利了，咱们就应该穿得好一点儿。
Money must be used for building (lit. on the side of building).	Qián yào yòng zài jiànshè fāngmiàn.	钱要用在建设方面。
What does it matter if we wear clothes that are a little old.	Yīfu chuān de jiù yìdiǎnr, yòu yǒu shénme guānxi ne?	衣服穿得旧一点儿，又有什么关系呢？
It's killer hot today, there's not even a bit of wind.	Jīntiān rè jíle, lián diǎnr fēng yě méiyǒu.	今天热极了，连点儿风也没有。
He's even learned it by heart, surely he reads it fluently.	Tā lián bèi dōu huì bèi le, yídìng niànde hěn liúlì.	他连背都会背了，一定念得很流利。
It's not ready/done yet. (food cooking)	Hái bù shú ne.	还不熟呢。
I haven't yet read today's paper.	Jīntiān de bào wǒ hái méi kàn ne.	今天的报我还没看呢。
I haven't even read the paper yet.	Wǒ lián bào hái méi kàn ne.	我连报还没看呢。
It doesn't matter if you don't give it back.	Bù huán méi guānxi.	不还没关系。
It's so far, how can he get back before 5?	Zhème yuǎn, wǔdiǎn yǐqián yòu zěnme néng huílái?	这么远，五点以前又怎么能回来？
The text isn't long, how many vocab items can it have!	Kèwén bù cháng, yòu néng yǒu duōshǎo shēngcí!	课文不长，又能有多少生词！
He's explained the text, but not yet the grammar.	Kèwén jiǎngwán le, yǔfǎ méi jiǎng ne.	课文讲完了，语法还没讲呢。
The map we already bought.	Dìtú yǐjīng mǎi le.	地图已经买了。
We've gotten the change too.	Zhǎo yě zhǎole.	找也找了。
Let's go back.	Wǒmen huíqu ba.	我们回去吧。
What time does the paper get delivered every day?	Bào měitiān jǐdiǎnzhōng sònglai?	报每天几点钟送来？
Are you coming or him?	Nǐ lái háishi tā lái?	你来，还是他来？
Are you coming or not?	Nǐ lái, háishi bù lái?	你来，还是不来？
Did you use a pen or a pencil?	Nǐ yòng de shi gāngbǐ, háishi qiānbǐ?	你用的是钢笔还是铅笔？
Let's go to the post office first and then go shopping.	Wǒmen xiān qù yóujú zài qù mǎi dōngxi ba.	我们先去邮局再去买东西吧。
You'd better go at 7. (not before)	Nǐ qīdiǎnzhōng zài qù ba.	你七点钟再去吧。
It's too late, better not go till tomorrow.	Tài wǎn le, míngtiān zài qù ba.	太晚了，明天再去吧。
Yesterday he called.	Zuótiān tā dǎ diànhuà lai.	昨天他打电话来。
He was chatting with two other friends.	Tā zhèng hé lìngwài liǎngwèi péngyou tánhuà.	他正和另外两位朋友谈话。
He introduced us to each other.	Tā gěi wǒmen hùxiāng jièshàole yíxiàr.	他给我们互相介绍了一下儿。
There were lots and lots of records on the table.	Zhuōzishang fàngzhe xǔduō chàngpiàn.	桌子上放着许多唱片。
This was given as a gift.	Zhè shi sòng de.	这是送的。
We listened to a symphony and a piano concerto.	Wǒmen tīng de shi jiāoxiǎngyuè hé gāngqín xiézòuqǔ.	我们听的是交响乐和钢琴协奏曲。
3 records	sān zhāng chàngpiàn	三张唱片
8 concerti	bā bù xiézòuqǔ	八部协奏曲
This is the Yellow River.	Zhè shi huánghé.	这是黄河。
This piece was composed in the last several years.	Zhè bù yīnyuè zuòpǐn shi zuìjìn jǐnián chuàngzuò de.	这部音乐作品是最近几年创作的。
It describes China's anti-Japanese war.	Nèiróng shi miáoxiě zhōngguó kàngrì zhànzhēng de.	内容是描写中国抗日战争的。
He introduced us to contemporary Peking opera.	Tā gěi wǒmen jièshàole zhōngguó xiàndài jīngjù.	他给我们介绍了中国现代京剧。
If you have time, we'd like to hear those other records.	Rúguǒ nǐ yǒu shíjiān, wǒmen hái xiǎng tīngting lìngwài nàxiē chàngpiàn.	如果你有时间，我们还想听听另外那些唱片。
You should completely read the vocabulary first and (only) then read the lesson.	Nǐ yīnggāi xiān niànshúle shēngcí, zài niàn kèwén.	你应该先念熟了生词，再念课文。
He says he'll finish eating before he goes.	Tā shuō tā chīwánfàn zài qù.	他说他吃完饭再去。
Tell him not to leave before 7.	Jiào tā qīdiǎnzhōng zài zǒu.	叫他七点钟再走。
I brought that magazine.	Wǒ bǎ nà běn zázhì dàilai le.	我把那本杂志带来了。
I've finished today's exercises.	Wǒ bǎ jīntiān de liànxí zuòwánle.	我把今天的练习作完了。
Please say a bit about your work experiences.	Qǐng nǐ bǎ nǐ de gōngzuò jīngyàn jièshaojieshao.	请你把你的工作经验介绍介绍。
Let's discuss those questions.	Zánmen bǎ nàxiē wèntí tǎolùn ba.	咱们把那些问题讨论吧。
I took his letter and put it on the table.	Wǒ bǎ tā de xìn fàng zài zhuōzishang le.	我把他的信放在桌子上了。
I still haven't finished that book, I'll give it back to you tomorrow.	Wǒ hái méi bǎ nàběn shū kànwán, míngtiān zài huán nǐ ba.	我还没把那本书看完，明天再还你吧。
We should memorize the new vocab.	Wǒmen yīnggāi bǎ shēngcí jìzhù.	我们应该把生词记住。
I want to learn Chinese well.	Wǒ yào bǎ zhōngwén xuéhǎo.	我要把中文学好。
We must give conveniences to others and keep difficulties for ourselves.	Wǒmen yào bǎ fāngbian rànggěi biéren, bǎ kùnnàn liúgěi zìjǐ.	我们要把方便让给别人，把困难留给自己。
We're going to see a movie, aren't we?	Wǒmen shìbushi qù kàn diànyǐng?	我们是不是去看电影？
You still haven't called him, huh?	Nǐ hái méi gěi tā dǎ diànhuà ne, shìbushi?	你还没给他打电话呢，是不是？
Haven't you already taken the patients to the hospital?	Shìbushi nǐ yǐjīng bǎ bìngrén sòngdào yīyuàn qu le?	是不是你已经把病人送到医院去了？

He's Canadian.	Tā shi jiānádà rén.	他是加拿大人。
He explained China's anti-Japanese war.	Tā jiǎngle zhōngguó de kàngrì zhànzhēng.	他讲了中国的抗日战争。
He deeply loved the people.	Tā rèaì rénmín.	他热爱人民。
He was absolutely selfless and thought only of others.	Tā háobùlìjǐ, zhuānménlìrén.	他毫不利己，专门利人。
He actively attended soldiers of the 8th Route Army.	Tā jījí gěi bālùjūn zhànshì kànbìng.	他积极给八路军战士看病。
A soldier suffered a serious wound.	Zhànshì shòule zhòngshāng.	战士受了重伤。
They carried him to the hospital.	Tāmen bǎ tā táidàole yīyuàn.	他们把他抬到了医院。
He had already fainted from losing too much blood.	Tā yīnwèi liúxuè tài duō, yǐjīng hūnmíle.	他因为流血太多，已经昏迷了。
His life was in great danger.	Shēngmìng fēicháng wēixiǎn.	生命非常危险。
Seeing things in this state, he went out.	Kàndào zhèzhǒng qíngkuàng, tā chūqule.	看到这种情况，他出去了。
Is it necessary to do a transfusion?	Shìbushi bìxū shūxuè?	是不是必须输血？
The hospital didn't have enough blood.	Yīyuànli de xuè bú gòu le.	医院里的血不够了。
Go ahead and draw my blood.	Chōu wǒ de xuè ba.	抽我的血吧。
He disagrees.	Tā bù tóngyì.	他不同意。
Work was so busy they couldn't let him transfuse blood.	Gōngzuò zhèyang máng, bù néng ràng tā shūxuè.	工作这样忙，不能让他输血。
In order to liberate the people he was wounded.	Wèile jiěfàng rénmín tā shòule shāng.	为了解放人民他受了伤。
We must certainly save his life.	Wǒmen yídìng yào bǎ tā jiùhuó.	我们一定要把他救活。
It is what should be done.	Shi yīnggāi de.	是应该的。
He lay down on the bed.	Tā tǎng zài chuángshang.	他躺在床上。
He gave it (as a transfusion) to the wounded comrade.	Tā shūgěile shòushāng de tóngzhì.	他输给了受伤的同志。
He is a great internationalist soldier.	Tā shi wěidà guójìzhǔyì zhànshì.	他是伟大国际主义战士。

Please talk a little about your experiences.	Qǐng nǐ bǎ nǐ de jīngyàn tántan.	请你把你的经验谈谈。
He bought that radio yesterday (and brought it here).	Tā zuótian bǎ nà jià shōuyīnjī mǎi lái le.	他昨天把那架收音机买来了。
He still hasn't finished writing the letter.	Tā hái méiyǒu bǎ xìn xiěwán.	他还没有把信写完。
Please put the things on the table.	Qǐng nǐ bǎ dōngxi fàng zài zhuōzi shang.	请你把东西放在桌子上。
He translated this sentence into English.	Tā bǎ zhège jùzi fānyìchéng yīngwén le.	他把这个句子翻译成英文了。
Did you give that book back to him?	Nǐ shìbushi bǎ nà běn shū huángěi tā le?	你是不是把那本书还给他了？
Did all the participants leave?	Shìbushi cānjiā de rén dōu zǒule?	是不是参加的人都走了？
He's thinking to listen to this symphony (once through).	Tā xiǎng bǎ zhèbù jiāoxiǎngyuè tīng yíbiàn.	他想把这部交响乐听一遍。
Several students are sitting under the big tree.	Dà shù xià zuòzhe jǐge xuéshēng.	大树下坐着几个学生。
The doctor told him to stay lying down.	Dàifu jiào tā tǎngzhe búyào qǐlái.	大夫叫他躺着不要起来。
The revolution was victorious.	Gémìng shèngdào le.	革命胜到了。
He came back to the dorm with quite a few letters.	Tā názhe hǎo jǐ fēng xìn huí sùshè lái le.	他拿着好几封信回宿舍来了。
It has to be done immediately.	Bìxū mǎshàng zuò.	必须马上作。
Otherwise his life may be in danger.	Bùrán huì yǒu shēngmìng wēixiǎn.	不然会有生命危险。
Should we eat now or in a little while?	Xiànzài chī, háishi yíhuìr chī?	现在吃还是一会儿吃？
The food's all made.	Fàncài dōu zuòhǎole.	饭菜都做好了。
With a little patching these two pieces of clothing can still be worn.	Zhè liǎng jiàn yīfu bǔyibu hái néng chuān ne.	这两件衣服补一补还能穿呢。
I thought the stamps were already used up.	Wǒ yǐwéi yóupiào yǐjīng yòngwánle.	我以为邮票已经用完了。
Two new students came to the class.	Bānshang láile liǎngge xīn xuéshēng.	班上来了两个新学生。
A few people got out of the car.	Qìchēshang xiàqùle yìxiē rén.	汽车上下了一些人。
Sometimes (he was) so busy he forgot to eat.	Yǒu shíhou máng de lián fàn yě wàngle chī.	有时候忙得连饭也忘了吃。
Before liberation, it was even hard for our family to eat.	Jiěfàng yǐqián, wǒmen jiā lián chīfàn dōu hěn kùnnan.	解放以前，我们家连吃饭都很困难。
It was hard to eat, where would we have money for books?	Chīfàn dōu hěn kùnnan, nǎr yǒu qián mǎi shū ne.	吃饭都很困难，哪儿有钱买书呢？
Even seven- and eight-year-olds love to do physical labor.	Lián qībāsuì de háizi dōu rèài láodòng.	连七八岁的孩子都热爱劳动。
He was burned while fighting a fire.	Tā jiùhuǒ de shíhou shāoshāngle.	他救火的时候烧伤了。
They put him in the hospital.	Tāmen bǎ tā sòngjinle yīyuàn.	他们把他送进了医院。
His wound was serious.	Tā shāng hěn zhòng.	他伤很重。
He passed through three hospitals, and only then was his life saved.	Tā jīngguo sānge yīyuàn, cái bǎ tā jiùhuóle.	他经过三个医院，才把他救活了。
Only with the great efforts of many doctors was his life saved.	Hǎo xiē dàifu de nǔlì, cái bǎ tā jiùhuóle.	好些大夫的努力，才把他救活了。
A burned child came to be admitted to the hospital.	Yīyuànli sònglaile yígè shāoshāng de háizi.	医院里送来了一个烧伤的孩子。
He's just recovered.	Tā gāng kāngfùle.	他刚康复了。
Draw as much (blood) as you want.	Yào duōshǎo jiù chōu duōshǎo.	要多少就抽多少。
Your wound is just healed.	Nǐ de shāng gāng hǎo.	你的伤刚好。
It will have an effect on your body.	Duì nǐ de shēntǐ yǒu yǐngxiǎng.	对你的身体有影响。
It's important to save the child.	Jiù háizi yàojǐn.	救孩子要紧。
The doctor tightly held his hand.	Dàifu jǐnjin de wò tā de shǒu.	大夫紧紧的喔他的手。
We should learn from his spirit.	Wǒmen yīnggāi xuéxí tā de jīngshén.	我们应该学习他的精神。
He's already been working in the factory for three years.	Tā zài gōngchǎng yǐjīng gōngzuòle sānniánle.	他在工厂已经工作了三年了。
We went to the park to hang out for a while.	Wǒmen dào gōngyuán wánrle yíhuìr.	我们到公园玩儿了一会儿。
It rained for more than an hour.	Yǔ xiàle yígeduō xiǎoshí.	雨下了一个多小时。
Did you review the text for two hours?	Nǐ fùxí kèwén fùxíle liǎngge xiǎoshí ma?	你复习课文复习了两个小时吗？
I only reviewed for an hour and a half.	Wǒ zhǐ fùxíle yígebàn xiǎoshí.	我只复习了一个半小时。
You've studied for more than half a year.	Nǐ xuéle bànniánduōle.	你学了半年多了。
He went to China two years ago?	Tā qù zhōngguó liǎngniánle ma?	他去中国两年了吗？
He didn't go to China two years ago, just over one year.	Tā qù zhōngguó méiyǒu liǎngnián, gāng yìniánduō.	他去中国没有两年，刚一年多。

For how many months have you been studing Chinese?	Nǐ xuéle jǐge yuè zhōngwén?	你学了几个月中文？
No, I don't review the lesson for an hour a day.	Bù, wǒ měitiān bù fùxí yíge xiǎoshí kèwén.	不，我每天不复习一个小时课文。
As soon as he got outside to look he saw it was snowing extremely heavily.	Tā dào wàibian yíkàn, xuě xiàde dàjíle.	他到外边一看，雪下得大极了。
As soon as I picked up the phone and listened, it was him.	Wǒ náqǐ diànhuà yìtīng, shi tā.	我拿起电话一听，是他。
As soon as he got to the store and asked, that kind he liked was sold out.	Tā dào shāngdiàn yíwèn, tā xǐhuan de nàzhǒng méiyǒu le.	他到商店一问，他喜欢的那种没有了。
Mom brought him and younger brother to the park to play for the day.	Māma dài tā hé dìdi dào gōngyuán wánrle yìtiān.	妈妈带他和弟弟到公园玩儿了一天。
There were peasants and PLA soldiers.	Yǒu nóngmín hé jiěfàngjūn.	有农民和解放军。
Some of the cadres were walking, some were rowing.	Gànbu yǒude sànbù, yǒude huáchuán.	干部有的散步，有的划船。
Some were sitting and chatting and drinking tea.	Yǒude zuòzhe tánhuà, hēchá.	有的坐着谈话，喝茶。
They went running to have a look.	Tāmen pǎoqu yí kàn.	他们跑去一看。
They saw a lot of people standing under a tree.	Tāmen kànjian shùxià zhànzhe hěn duō rén.	他们看见树下站着很多人。
They were giving everyone a performance.	Tāmen zhèngzài gěi dàjiā biǎoyǎn jiémù ne.	他们正在给大家表演节目呢。
He danced.	Tā tiàowǔle.	他跳舞了。
He watched for more than half an hour.	Tā kànle bàngeduō xiǎoshí.	他看了半个多小时。
Dad showed them how for a while.  (e.g. to row)	Bàba jiāole tāmen yíhuìr.	爸爸教了他们一会儿。
He didn't feel even a bit tired.	Tā yìdiǎnr yě bù juéde lèi.	他一点儿也不觉得累。
When they finished rowing, they went to climb a hill.	Huáwán chuán, tāmen yòu qù pá shān.	划完船，他们又去爬山。
The red wall was beautiful.	Hóng qiáng hǎokàn jíle.	红墙好看极了。
In that place there wasn't yet even a single tree.	Nàge dìfang hái yìkē shù dōu méiyǒu ne.	那个地方还一棵树都没有呢。
Now it's all planted over with trees.	Xiànzài dōu zhòngshang shù le.	现在都种上树了。
These buildings were built by workers hundreds of years ago.	Zhè xiē jiànzhù shi jǐ bǎi nián qián láodòng rénmín xiūjiànde.	这些建筑是几百年前劳动人民修建的。
If it weren't for their labor, we couldn't have this kind of park.	Yàoshi méiyǒu tāmen de láodòng, jiù bú huì yǒu zhèyang de gōngyuán.	要是没有他们的劳动，就不会有这样的公园。
He added: "Before liberation they rarely came to hang out."	Tā jiēzhe shuō: "Jiěfàng yǐqián tāmen hěn shǎo lái wánr."	他接着说：＂解放以前他们很少来玩儿。＂
The park has become the workers' own.	Gōngyuán chéngle láodòng rénmín zìjǐ de le.	公园成了劳动人民自己的了。
A great change has occurred.	Fāshēngle hěn dà de biànhuà.	发生了很大的变化。
The blue sky is pretty.	Lántiān hǎokàn.	蓝天好看。
We've haven't yet studied for two years.	Wǒmen xuéxíle hái búdào liǎngnián ne.	我们学习了还不到两年呢。
It'll soon be two years that he's worked at this school.	Tā zài zhège xuéxiào gōngzuò kuài liǎngnián le.	他在这个学校工作快两年了。
He graduated two years ago.	Tā bìyè liǎngnián le.	他毕业两年了。
It's already a year since he went to China.	Tā qù zhōngguó yǐjīng yìnián le.	他去中国已经一年了。
As soon as he said it everyone laughed.	Tā yìshuō, dàjiā dōu xiào le.	他一说，大家都笑了。
He came running into the factory.	Tā pǎo jìn gōngchǎng láile.	他跑进工厂来了。
He took the book down (to us).	Tā bǎ shū náxialai le.	他把书拿下来了。
They sent the new student back.	Xīn xuéshēng tāmen sònghuiqu le.	新学生他们送回去了。
I saw them walk across.	Wǒ kànjian tāmen zǒuguoqu le.	我看见他们走过去了。
He stands up and greets his friends.	Tā zhànqilai gēn péngyoumen dǎ zhāohu.	他站起来跟朋友们打招呼。
He had me come sit down.	Tā ràng wǒ zuòxialai.	他让我坐下来。
He quickly climbed up the hill.	Tā kuài páshang shān qu le.	他快爬上山去了。
He bought/brought back stamps.	Tā mǎihui yóupiào lai le.	他买回邮票来了。
Please send the dictionary back to the library.	Qǐng nǐ bǎ zìdiǎn sònghui túshūguǎn qu ba.	请你把字典送回图书馆去吧。
He takes several pictorials down from the shelf.	Ta cóng shūjiàshang náxialai jǐběn huàbào.	他从书架上拿下来几本画报。
I'll wrap these things up right away.	Wǒ mǎshàng bǎ zhèxiē dōngxi bāohǎo.	我马上把这些东西包好。
You have to wait for the bus at that bus stop.	 Nǐ yào zài nàge qìchēzhàn děng chē.	你要在那个汽车站等车。
When I get time I'll definitely go.	Děng yǒu shíjiān wǒ yídìng qù.	等有时间我一定去。
I'll come in a minute.	Wǒ děng yìhuǐr jiù lái.	我等一会儿就来。
We go as soon as we wake up.	Wǒmen yì qǐlái jiù qù.	我们一起来就去。
As soon as I got here he welcomed me.	Wǒ yí dào zhèli, tā jiù huānying wǒ.	我一到这里，他就欢迎我。
He notices our pronunciation is wrong.	Tā fāxiàn wǒmen de fāyīn cuò le.	他发现我们的发音错了。
He immediately has me correct it.	Tā lìkè ràng wǒ gǎizhèng.	他立刻让我改正。
As soon as the weather gets cold we can go skating.	Tiānqi yì lěng, wǒmen jiù kěyi qù huábīng le.	天气一冷，我们就可以去滑冰了。
The minute I don't pay attention I'm liable to read wrong.	Wǒ yí bu zhùyì jiù huì niàncuò.	我一不注意就会念错。
He runs and jumps his way to school.	Tā yòu pǎo yòu tiào de qù shàngxué.	他又跑又跳地去上学。
The sun was just coming out.	Tàiyang gāng chūlai.	太阳刚出来。
She discovered that there was a small paper package in the grass by the side of the road.	Tā fāxiàn lùpáng de cǎoli yǒu yíge xiǎo zhǐ baō.	她发现路旁的草里有一个小纸包。
five roads	wǔ tiáo lù	五条路
He picked up an envelope.	Tā jiǎnqilaile yíge xìnfēng.	他捡起来了一个信封。
Fifty dollars was enclosed.	Lǐbian zhuāngzhe wǔshí kuài qián.	里边装着五十块钱。
The guy who lost the money is probably Chinese.	Diū qián de rén dàgài shi zhōngguó rén.	丢钱的人大概是中国人。
I return the money to him.	Wǒ bǎ qián jiāogěi tā.	我把钱交给他。
Perhaps he will come back to look for it.	Tā yěxǔ huì huílai zhǎo de.	他也许会回来找的。
An old gentlemen came walking up.	Yíge lǎodàye zǒuguolai le.	一个老大爷走过来了。
He was walking and looking at the ground.	Tā yìbiān zǒu yìbiān wǎng dìshang kàn.	他一边走一边往地上看。
Yes, young lady.	Shì a, xiǎo gūniang.	是啊，小姑娘。
The commune had me come to the city to repair machinery.	Shèli pài wǒ dào chéngli lái xiūlǐ jīqi.	社里派我到城里来修理机器。
I just this moment delivered the machines to the factory.	Wǒ gāngcái bǎ jīqi sòngdao gōngchǎng qu le.	我刚才把机器送到工厂去了。
He took the paper package (that she handed him).	Tā jiēguo zhǐ bāo.	他接过纸包。

seven pieces of business	qī jiàn shì	七件事
They came walking in from outside.	Tāmen cóng wàibian zǒujinlaile.	他们从外边走进来了。
He picks up a paper and comes and sits down to read it.	Tā náqi yìzhāng bào lái, zuò xià lái kàn.	他拿起一张报来，坐下来看。
Two points need to be kept in mind.	Yǒu liǎng diǎn yào zhùyì.	有两点要注意。
He's going to bring a chair up from downstairs.	Tā yào cóng lóuxià náshang yì bǎ yǐzi lái.	他要从楼下拿上一把椅子来。
As soon as we got off the plane we drove to the embassy.	Wǒmen yí xià fēijī jiù zuò qìchē dào dàshǐguǎn qù le.	我们一下飞机就坐汽车到大使馆去了。
As soon as we heard it we understood.	Wǒmen yì tīng jiù dǒngle.	我们一听就懂了。
Don't get tense.	Bú yào jǐnzhāng.	不要紧张。
As soon as you get tense you'll read it wrong.	Nǐ yì jǐnzhāng jiù huì niàn cuò.	你一紧张就会念错。
As soon as you speak fast I don't understand.	Nǐ shuō de yí kuài, wǒ jiù tīngbudǒng le.	你说得一快，我就听不懂了。
Before he didn't know even a single character.	Yǐqián tā yíge hànzì yě bú rènshi.	以前他一个汉字也不认识。
I haven't visited that chemical factory even once.	Nàge huàxué gōngchǎng wǒ yícì yě méi cānguānguo.	那个化学工厂我一次也没参观过。
There wasn't even a single person in the dorm.	Sùshèli yíge rén yě méiyǒu.	宿舍里一个人也没有。
When he got out of the hospital, he came to class without even a single day's rest.	Tā chūle yuàn, yì tiān dōu méi xiūxi, jiù lái shàngkè le.	他出了院，一天都没休息，就来上课了。
Those sentences aren't a bit hard.	Nàxiē jùzi yìdiǎnr dōu bù nán.	那些句子一点儿都不难。
I participated in the meet and I'm a bit tired.	Wǒ cānjiāle yùndònghuì, yǒu diǎnr leì.	我参加了运动会，有点儿累。
Now I can a little (e.g. skate).	Wǒ xiànzài yǒu diǎnr huì le.	我现在有点儿会了。
We were a little unaccustomed to the weather there.	Wǒmen duì nàr de tiānqi yǒudiǎnr bù xíguàn.	我们对那儿的天气有点儿不习惯。
The weather's gotten a bit cold.	Tiānqi yǒu diǎnr lěng le.	天气有点儿冷了。
We should change into something a little thicker.	Wǒmen yīnggāi huàn hòu diǎnr de yīfu le.	我们应该换厚点儿的衣服了。
The meet takes place on Saturday.	Yùndònghuì shi xīngqīliù jǔxíng de.	运动会是星期六举行的。
I'm participating in the all-city college meet.	Wǒ cānjiā quánshì dàxuéshēng yùndònghuì.	我参加全市大学生运动会。
The competition goes on for four hours.	Bǐsài jìnxíng sìge xiǎoshí.	比赛进行四个小时。
I took part in the high jump competition.	Wǒ cānjiāle tiào gāo bǐsài.	我参加了跳高比赛。
1.70 meters	yì mǐ qī líng	一米七零
Just when I was feeling a lack of confidence, he came.	Wǒ zhèng gǎndào méiyǒu xìnxīn de shíhou, tā láile.	我正感到没有信心的时候，他来了。
A competitor (at the meet) came and gave me a glass of water.	Yíge yùndòngyuán gěi wǒ sòngláile yìbēi shǔi.	一个运动员给我送来了一杯水。
This may affect your achievement.	Zhè huì yǐngxiǎng nǐ de chéngji de.	这会影响你的成绩的。
Competition is not the point.	Bǐsài bú shi mùdì.	比赛不是目的。
The most important thing is, through competition, to strengthen unity.	Zuì zhòngyào de shi tōngguò bǐsài jiāqiáng tuánjié.	最重要的是通过比赛加强团结。
The most important thing is to promote friendship.	Zuì zhòngyào de shi zēngjìn yǒuyì.	最重要的是增进友谊。
Come on, let's practice.	Lái, zánmen liànxí ba.	来，咱们练习吧。
I finally cleared 1.80 meters.	Wǒ zhōngyú tiàoguole yìmǐbālíng.	我终于跳过了一米八零。
The competition came to an end.	Bǐsài jiéshùle.	比赛结束了。

It's still early.	Shíjiān hái zǎo.	时间还早。
He wasn't a bit nervous.	Tā yìdiǎnr yě bù jǐnzhāng.	他一点儿也不紧张。
That word's used a bit wrong.	Nàge cí yòng de yǒu diǎnr bù héshì.	那个词用得有点儿不合适。
These two characters are written a bit small.	Zhè liángge zì xiěde yǒu diǎnr xiǎo.	这两个字写得有点儿小。
I just started learning how to ride a bike.	Wǒ gāng xué qí zìxíngchē.	我刚学骑自行车。
The trees have turned a bit green.	Shù yǒu diǎnr lǜ le.	树有点儿绿了。
He's in good health.	Tā shēntǐ hěn hǎo.	他身体很好。
His resolution is great.	Tā juéxīn fēicháng dà.	他决心非常大。
The sound of this kind of TV isn't bad.	Zhèzhǒng diànshì shēngyin búcuò.	这种电视声音不错。
Can you hear clearly or not?	Nǐ tīng de qīngchu tīng bu qīngchu?	你听得清楚听不清楚？
We can't read these books.	Zhèxiē shū wǒmen kànbudǒng.	这些书我们看不懂。
Can this number be performed in 20 minutes?	Zhège jiémù èrshífēnzhōng biǎoyǎn de wán ma?	这个节目二十分钟表演得完吗？
If we don't review a few more times we won't remember.	Bùduō fùxí jǐcì jiù jìbuzhù.	不多复习几次就记不住。
Can you move this bed by yourself?	Zhè zhāng chuáng nǐ yíge rén bāndeqǐ bānbuqǐ?	这张床你一个人搬得起搬不起？
Will you be able to go?	Nǐ qùdeliǎo qùbuliǎo?	你去得了去不了？
There's not enough time.	Shíjiān bú gòu.	时间不够。
We can't discuss three questions (e.g. not enough time left).	Tǎolùnbuliǎo sānge wèntí le.	讨论不了三个问题了。　
It's gotten too warm, we can't skate any more.	Tài nuǎnhuo le, huábuliǎo bīng le.	太暖和了，滑不了冰了。
He won't be able to move that table by himself.	Tā yíge rén bānbudòng nàzhāng zhuōzi.	他一个人搬不动那张桌子。
Let's go help him carry it (the table).	Wǒmen qù bāngzhu tā tái ba.	我们去帮助他抬吧。
Old people won't be strong enough to go by foot.	Lǎo rén zǒubudòng.	老人走不动。
They'll go by car.	Tāmen zuò chē qù.	他们坐车去。
Can you carry so many things?	Zhème duō dōngxi nǐ nádedòng ma?	这么多东西你拿得动吗？
Is this dorm room big enough for three people?	Zhè jiān sùshè zhùdexià zhùbuxià sānge rén?	这间宿舍住得下住不下三个人？
This little boat only seats four.	Zhè zhī xiǎo chuán zhǐ zuòdexià sì ge rén.	这只小船只坐得下四个人。
It seats four, five won't fit.	Zuòdexià sìge rén, wǔge rén jiù zuòbuxià le.	坐得下四个人，五个人就坐不下了。
Can this many books fit on the shelf?	Shūjiàshang fàngdexià zhème duō shū ma?	书架上方得下这么多书吗？
There's no more room to put these photos in the envelope.	Xìnfēngli zhuāngbuxià zhè xiē zhàopiàn le.	信封里装不下这些照片了。
We want to constantly improve our Chinese.	Wǒmen yào búduàn tígāo zhōngwén shǔipíng.	我们要不断提高中文水平。
He wanted to meet a friend at the station, so he left early.	Tā yào qù chēzhàn jiē yíge péngyou, zǎozāor de jiù zǒule.	他要去车站接一个朋友，早早儿地就走了。
Several books were placed neatly on the table.	Zhuōzishang zhěngzhěngqíqí de fàngzhe jǐběn shū.	桌子上整整齐齐地方着几本书。
It's getting colder by the day.	Tiānqi yuèlái yuèlěng.	天气越来越冷。
The more he listened to this symphony the more he liked listening to it.	Zhè bù jiāoxiǎngyuè tā yuètīng yuèxǐhuantīng.	这部交响乐他越听越喜欢听。
The more I think about it, the more I feel this story is interesting.	Wǒ yuèxiǎng yuèjuéde zhège gùshi yǒu yìsi.	我越想越觉得这个故事有意思。
fable	yùyán	寓言
In ancient times there was a man who everyone called Foolish Old Man.	Gǔ shíhou yǒu yíwèi rén, gèjiào yúgōng.	古时候有一位人，各叫愚公。
He was nearly 90.	Tā kuài jiǔshísuì le.	他快九十岁了。
In front of his doors were two mountains.	Tā de mén qiánbian yǒu liǎngzuò shān.	他的门前边有两座山。
He called all the people of the house together.	Tā bǎ quán jiā rén jiàodào yìqǐ.	他把全家人叫到一起。
Having these two mountains facing our doorway is very inconvenient.	Zhè liǎngzuò shān duìzhe zánmen jiā ménkǒu tài bù fāngbiàn le.	这两座山对着咱们家门口太不方便了。
Let's move it away.	Zánmen bǎ tā bānzǒu ba.	咱们把它搬走吧。
His son and grandsons were all much in favor.	Tā de érzi, sūnzimen dōu hěn zànchéng.	他的儿子，孙子们都很赞成。
Only his wife lacked confidence.	Zhǐ yǒu tā de qīzi méiyǒu xìnxīn.	只有他的妻子没有信心。
Your age is so great, you can't move a single stone.	Nǐ niánji zhème dàle, lián yíkuài shítou yě bānbudòng.	你年纪这么大了，连一块石头也搬不动。
And where are you going to move so many stones to?	Zhème duō de shítou yòu bāndào nǎr qù ne?	这么多的石头又搬到哪儿去呢？
We can go throw the stones in the ocean.	Wǒmen kěyi bǎ shítou rēngdào hǎili qu.	我们可以把石头扔到海里去。
He took the whole family to move the mountain.	Tā dàizhe yìjiā rén bān shān qu le.	他带着一家人搬山去了。
Next door was a seven or eight-year-old kid.	Línjū yǒu ge qībāsuì de háizi.	邻居有个七八岁的孩子。
They did not fear hardship.	Tāmen bú pà xīnkǔ.	他们不怕辛苦。
Every day they unceasingly dug the mountain.	Měitiān búduàn wā shān.	每天不断挖山。
There was an old man named Wise Old Man.	Yǒu ge lǎotóuzi jiào zhìsǒu.	有个老头子叫智叟。
He felt it was ridiculous.	Tā juéde hěn hǎoxiào.	他觉得很好笑。
You're so old, you can't even pluck the grass.	Nǐ zhème dà niánji, lián cǎo dōu bábuliǎo.	你这么大年纪，连草都拔不了。
You're still not as good as a child.	Nǐ hái bùrú xiǎoháizi.	你还不如小孩子。
Although I'll die soon, I have sons.	Wǒ suīrán kuài sǐle, dànshi wǒ hái yǒu érzi.	我虽然快死了，但是我还有儿子。
When he heard that, he had nothing to say.	Tīngle, méiyǒu huà shuō.	听了，没有话说。
It moved God.	Gǎndòng le shàngdì.	感动了上帝。
He sent two fairies to move the mountain away.	Tā pàile liǎng ge shénxiān bǎ shān bān zǒu le.	他派了两个神仙把山搬走了。
The color in that movie is excellent.	Nà bù diànyǐng sècǎi fēicháng hǎo.	那部电影色彩非常好。
He was able to find it.	Tā zhǎo de dào.	他找得到。
Will you be able to come at 7?	Nǐ qīdiǎnzhōng láideliǎo láibuliǎo?	你七点钟来得了来不了。
You don't need to go. (i.e. the two of us can handle it)	Nǐ búyòng qù le.	你不用去了。
The two of us can carry that machine.	Wǒmen liǎngge rén táidedòng nà jià jīqì.	我们两个人抬的动那架机器。
He got too tired climbing the mountain, afterward he couldn't walk.	Tā pá shān pá de tài lèi le, hòulái zǒu bu dòng le.	他爬山爬得太累了，后来走不动了。
That bus seats forty.	Nà liàng qìchē zuòdexià sìshí ge rén.	那辆汽车坐得下四十个人。
There's not room to put so many things in here.	Zhèlǐ fàngbúxià zhème duō dōngxi.	这里放不下这么多东西。
As time goes on I have more and more friends.	Wǒ de péngyou yuèlái yuèduō le.	我的朋友越来越多了。
The life of the commune member keeps getting better.	Shèyuán shēnghuó yuèlái yuèhǎo.	社员生活越来越好。
There's no water to drink.	Méiyǒu shǔi hē.	没有水喝。
There is land to cultivate.	Yǒu dì zhòng.	有地种。
We planted a lot of trees by the side of the dining hall.	Wǒmen zài shítáng pángbiān zhòngshangle hěn duō shù.	我们在食堂旁边种上了很多树。
Please write your names on your notebooks.	Qǐng nǐ zài běnzishang xiěshang zìjǐ de míngzi.	请你在本子上写上自己的名字。
He puts on his best looking clothes.	Tā chuānshang zuì hǎokàn de yīfu.	他穿上最好看的衣服。
We finally got to listen to that symphony.	Nà bù jiāoxiǎngyuè wǒmen zhōngyú tīngshang le.	那部交响乐我们终于听上了。
Yesterday they said it would rain today. (i.e. on the radio)	Zuótiān guǎngbō shuō jīntiān yǒu yǔ.	昨天广播说今天有雨。
They said it would rain today and in fact it's raining now.	Tāmen shuō jīntiān yǒu yǔ, xiànzài guǒrán xiàyǔ le.	他们说今天有雨，现在果然下雨了。
I figured it was him calling and, in fact, it was.	Wǒ xiǎng dàgài shi tā dǎlai de diànhuà, guǒrán shi tā.	我想大概是他打来的电话，果然是他。
He said it was really not bad and, in fact, that program was good.	Tā shuō hěn búcuò, nàge jiémù guǒrán hěn hǎo.	他说很不错，那个节目果然很好。
This auditorium sure is big.	Zhège lǐtáng jiùshi dà.	这个礼堂就是大。
In learning a foreign language you really have to talk a lot.	Xuéxí wàiwén jiùshi yào duō shuō, duō shuō.	学习外文就是要多说，多说。
He really likes to listen to music.	Tā jiùshi xǐhuan tīng yīnyuè.	他就是喜欢听音乐。
An army corps passed by the edge of a village.	Yì zhī bùduì cóng yīge cūnzi pángbiān jīngguò.	一支部队从一个村子旁边经过。
One night he came home.	Yì tiān yèli tā huíjiā láile	一天夜里他回家来了。
Because the sky was so dark they didn't see the road clearly.	Yīnwèi tiān tài hēi, kànbuqīng lù.	因为天太黑，看不清路。
A soldier stepped on a cabbage on the side of the field.	Yíge zhànshì bǎ dì biānrshang de yìkē báicài cǎihuàile.	一个战士把地边儿上的一棵白菜踩坏了。
He reported the matter to the squad leader right away.	Tā mǎshàng bǎ zhèjiàn shì bàogàole bānzhǎng.	他马上把这件事报告了班长。
He immediately called to mind the discipline of the PLA.	Tā lìkè xiǎngdào rénmín jiěfàngjūn de jìlǜ.	他立刻想到人民解放军的纪律。
We are the people's army.	Wǒmen shi rénmín de jūnduì.	我们是人民的军队。
We must whole-heartedly serve the people.	Yào quánxīnquányì wèi rénmín fúwù.	要全心全意为人民服务。
We must in all respects keep in mind the people's interest.	Yào chùchù xiǎngdào rénmín de lìyì.	要处处想到人民的利益。
We must certainly compensate (them for it).	Wǒmen yídìng yào péi.	我们一定要赔。
The people of the village were all asleep.	Cūnzili de rén dōu shuìle.	村子里的人都睡了。
They couldn't find anyone.	Yíge rén yě zhǎobudào.	一个人也找不到。
He asked everyone to think of a way (to handle the situation).	Tā ràng dàjiā xiǎng bànfǎ.	他让大家想办法。
We apologize to them.	Wǒmen xiàng tāmen dàoqiàn.	我们向他们道歉。
We compensate them for their loss.	Wǒmen péi tāmen de sǔnshi.	我们赔他们的损失。
The next day the commune members arrived at the field to work.	Dìèrtiān, shèyuán dào dìli láodòng.	第二天，社员到地里劳动。
Close the door on your way out.	Nǐ chūqu de shíhou bǎ mén guānshang.	你出去的时候把门关上。
I put some photos in the letter for my friend.	Wǒ zài gěi péngyou de xìnli zhuāngshangle jǐ zhāng zhàopiàn.	我在给朋友的信里装上了几张照片。
After liberation, the workers all lived a happy life.	Jiěfàng yǐhòu láodòng rénmín dōu guòshangle xìngfú shēnghuó.	解放以后劳动人民都过上了幸福生活。
There are a huge number of people who want to see that movie;  I still haven't managed to see it.	Yào kàn nàge diànyǐng de rén fēicháng duō, wǒ hái méi kànshang ne.	要看那个电影的人非常多，我还没看上呢。
He said he'd come at 7 and at 7 he did come.	Tā shuō qīdiǎn lái, qīdiǎn tā guǒrán láile.	他说七点来，七点他果然来了。
We sure don't fear difficulties.	Wǒmen jiùshi bú pà kùnnan.	我们就是不怕困难。

I can't hear.	Wǒ tīngbujiàn.	我听不见。
How many years did you live in Beijing?	Nǐ zài běijīng zhùle jǐnián?	你在北京住了几年？
How long do you listen to the radio?	Nǐ tīng duōshǎo shíjian de guǎngbō?	你听多少时间的广播？
We waited for you for more than 20 minutes.	Wǒmen děngle nǐ èrshí duō fēn zhōng le.	我们等了你二十多分钟了。
The sun will be out soon.	Tàiyang kuài chūlai le.	太阳快出来了。
The meet will end at 5.	Yùndònghuì wǔdiǎn zhōng jiùyào jiéshù le.	运动会五点钟就要结束了。
I still can't understand all of it (when I listen).	Wǒ hái bù néng dōu tīngdǒng.	我还不能都听懂。
In the evening I'm busy, I won't be able to attend.	Wǎnshàng wǒ yǒu shìqing, cānjiā bu liǎo.	晚上我有事情，参加不了。
I'll definitely be able to find the lost money.	Diū de qián wǒ yídìng zhǎo de dào.	丢的钱我一定找得到。
When studying a foreign language, if you don't speak often you won't speak fluently.	Xué wàiwén bù cháng shuō jiù shuō bù liúlì.	学外文不常说就说不流利。
This classroom has big windows.	Zhè jiān jiàoshì chuānghu hěn dà.	这间教室窗户很大。
He didn't write a single character from this lesson wrong.	Zhè kè hànzì tā yíge yě méiyǒu xiě cuò.	这课汉字他一个也没有写错。
They're all lent out. (eg. library's magazines)	Dōu jièzǒu le.	都借走了。
There's not even a single pictorial left.	Yìběn huàbào yě méiyǒu le.	一本画报也没有了。
It's the same with him as with us, he hasn't come here even a single time.	Tā gēn wǒmen yíyàng, zhèr yícì yě méi láiguo.	他跟我们一样，这儿一次也没来过。
He knows nothing at all about this matter.	Zhè jiàn shìqing tā yìdiǎnr dōu bù zhīdào.	这件事情他一点儿都不知道。
Four or five thousand years ago, a great flood occurred in China.	Sì, wǔ qiān nián yǐqián, zhōngguó fāshēngle yícì hěn dà de shuǐzāi.	四，五千年以前，中国发生了一次很大的水灾。
The great water flooded many places.	Dà shuǐ bǎ hǎo xiē dìfang dōu yānle.	大水把好些地方都淹了。
He leads everyone to harness the water.	Tā dàilǐng dàjiā qù zhìshuǐ.	他带领大家去治水。
They didn't balk at hardship or fatigue.	Tāmen bú pà xīnkǔ, bú pà lèi.	他们不怕辛苦，不怕累。
Their determination overcomes all difficulties.	Juéxīn kèfú gè zhǒng kùnnan.	决心克服各种困难。
They diverted the water to the sea.	Tāmen bǎ shuǐ yǐn dào hǎili qù.	他们把水引到海里去。
Many people's houses were flooded.	Hěn duō rén de jiā dōu yānle.	很多人的家都淹了。
He passed the doors of his own house.	Tā jīngguò zìjǐ jiā ménkǒu.	他经过自己家门口。
Our work thus wouldn't be accomplished.	Wǒmen de gōngzuò jiù wánchéng bu liǎo le.	我们的工作就完成不了了。
He still didn't go back.	Tā hái shi méiyǒu huíqù.	他还是没有回去。
While they were busy harnessing the water, 13 years of hard work passed.	Tāmen mángzhe zhìshuǐ, jīngguo shí sān nián de nǔlì.	他们忙着治水，经过十三年的努力。
My notebook and his aren't the same.	Wǒ de běnzi gēn tā de bù yíyàng.	我的本子跟他的不一样。
For us, being here is just like being at home.	Wǒmen zài zhèr jiù gēn zài zìjǐ jiāli yíyàng.	我们在这儿就跟在自己家里一样。
I'm thinking to buy a pen the same as that one of yours.	Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yìzhī gēn nǐ nàzhī yíyàng de gāngbǐ.	我想买一枝跟你那枝一样的钢笔。
Just like you, he especially likes listening to music.	Tā gēn nǐ yíyàng tèbié xǐhuan tīng yīnyuè.	他跟你一样特别喜欢听音乐。
He speaks Chinese as fluently as a Chinese person.	Tā shuō zhōngwén shuō de gēn zhōngguórén yíyàng liúlì.	他说中文说得跟中国人一样流利。
Going to the commune to do physical labor is a good opportunity to exercise.	Dào gōngshè qù láodòng shi shòu duànliàn de hǎo jīhuì.	到公社去劳动是受锻炼的好机会。
The snow on the ground was completely blown away by the wind.	Dìshang de xuě bèi fēng guā de yìdiǎnr yě méiyǒule.	地上的雪被风刮得一点儿也没有了。
That seriously wounded soldier was saved by the doctor.	Nàge shòu zhòng shāng de zhànshì jiào dàifu jiùhuó le.	那个受重伤的战士叫大夫救活了。
Those records have been lent out.	Nàxiē chàngpiàn ràng rén jièzǒule.	那些唱片让人借走了。
The invading army has all been driven out.	Qīnlüè jūn dōu bèi gǎnchuqu le.	侵略军都被赶出去了。
The difficulties can all be overcome by us.	Kùnnan dōu huì bèi wǒmen kèfú de.	困难都会被我们克服的。
This new kind of product was extremely well received.	Zhè zhǒng xīn chǎnpǐn fēicháng shòu huānyíng.	这种新产品非常受欢迎。
This old worker's practical experience exceeds ours.	Zhège lǎo gōngrén de shíjiàn jīngyàn bǐ wǒmen duō.	这个老工人的实践经验比我们多。
He knows even more about Beijing than I do.	Tā bǐ wǒ gèng liǎojiě běijīng de qíngkuàng.	他比我更了解北京的情况。
He walks much faster than I do.	Tā zǒu de bǐ wǒ kuài de duō.	他走得比我快得多。
His writing is a bit better than mine.	Tā de zì xiě de bǐ wǒ hǎo yìdiǎnr.	他的字写得比我好一点儿。
Class I has three fewer students than Class II.	Dìyī bān de xuéshēng bǐ dìèr shǎo sānge.	第一班的学生比第二少三个。
Production level is up a lot from last year.	Jīnnián de shēngchǎn shǔipíng bǐ qùnián tígāole hěn duō.	今年的生产水平比去年提高了很多。
This factory is not as big as that one.	Zhège gōngchǎng méiyǒu nàge gōngchǎng dà.	这个工厂没有那个工厂大。
This lesson's text isn't harder than that one's.	Zhèkè de kèwén bù bǐ nàkè nán.	这课的课文不比那课难。
It's getting warmer day by day.	Tiānqi yìtiān bǐ yìtiān nuǎnhuo le.	天气一天比一天暖和了。
These trees get taller every year.	Zhè xiē shù yìnián bǐ yìnián gāo.	这些树一年比一年高。
(The trees have) already gotten a good bit taller than this building.	Yǐjīng bǐ zhèzuò lóu gāo hǎo duō le.	已经比这座楼高好多了。
He's studied Chinese two years more than me.	Tā bǐ wǒ duō xuéle liǎngnián zhōngwén.	他比我多学了两年中文。
We've learned less than they have.	Wǒmen xuéde bǐ tāmen shǎo.	我们学得比他们少。
We've learned many fewer characters than they have.	Wǒmen bǐ tāmen shǎo xué hěn duō hànzì.	我们比他们少学很多汉字。
They came ten minutes earlier than we did.	Tāmen bǐ wǒmen zǎo láile shífēnzhōng.	他们比我们早来了十分钟。
I woke up a quarter of an hour later today than yesterday.	Wǒ jīntiān bǐ zuótiān wǎn qǐle yíkèzhōng.	我今天比昨天晚起了一刻钟。
I have an older brother and an older sister.	Wǒ yǒu gēge hé jiějie.	我有哥哥和姐姐。
My younger sister lives in Shanghai.	Wǒ mèimei zhù zài shànghǎi.	我妹妹住在上海。
Like other workers, he was exploited.	Tā gēn biéde gōngrén yíyàng shòu bōxuē.	他跟别的工人一样受剥削。
He was oppressed.	Tā shòu yāpò.	他受压迫。
His life was very hard.	Tā shēnghúo hěn kǔ.	他生活很苦。
He had to labor 16 or 17 hours in the factory.	Tā yào zài gōngchǎng láodòng shíliùqīge xiǎoshí.	他要在工厂劳动十六七个小时。
Once my father was fatigued to the point of illness.	Yǒu yícì wǒ bàba lèibìngle.	有一次我爸爸累病了。
He didn't have money for treatment.	Tā méi qián zhì.	他没钱治。
His illness got more serious by the day.	Tā bìng yìtiān bǐ yìtiān zhòng.	他病一天比一天重。
Finally he was driven out of the factory.	Zuìhòu bèi gǎnchule gōngchǎng.	最后被赶出了工厂。
He was working (as a laborer) at another factory.	Tā zài lìngwài yíge gōngchǎng láodòng.	他在另外一个工厂劳动。
He too was taken ill.	Tā yě bèi dǎ de bìngle.	他也被打得病了。
On being liberated, laborers were made the country's masters.	Jiěfàngle, láodòngrénmín zuòle guójiā de zhǔrén.	解放了，劳动人民做了国家的主人。
He was chosen by everyone to be made the factory's head cadre.	Tā bèi dàjiā xuǎnzuò gōngchǎng de lǐngdǎo gànbu.	他被大家选做工厂的领导干部。
He joined the PLA.	Tā cānjiāle jiěfàngjūn.	他参加了解放军。
He's not as old as I am.	Tā méiyǒu wǒ dà.	他没有我大。
My younger sister is two years younger than I am.	Mèimei bǐ wǒ xiǎo liǎng suì.	妹妹比我小两岁。
Like me, she goes to middle school.	Tā gēn wǒ yíyàng, dōu shàng zhōngxué.	她跟我一样，都上中学。
You must remember: if not for Chairman Mao we couldn't have today's happy life.	Nǐ yào jìzhù, méiyǒu máozhǔxí, jiù búhuì yǒu jīntiān de xìngfú shēnghuó.	你要记住：没有毛主席就不会有今天的幸福生活。
The most important thing is the leadership of the Chinese Communist Party.	Zuì zhòngyào de shi zhōngguó gòngchǎndǎng de lǐngdǎo.	最重要的是中国共产党的领导。

He writes the same as you.	Tā de zì xiě gēn nǐ de yíyàng.	他的字写跟你的一样。
My clothes are not the same length as yours.	Wǒ de yīfu gēn nǐ de yīfu bù yíyàng cháng.	我的衣服跟你的衣服不一样长。
This word's meaning isn't the same as that one's.	Zhège cí de yìsi bù gēn nàge cí yíyàng.	这个词的意思不跟那个词一样。
He was chosen people's representative by his comrades.	Tā bèi tóngzhìmén xuǎnzuò rénmín dàibiǎo le.	他被同志们选做人民代表了。
The picture on the wall will be blown down by the wind.	Qiángshang de huàr yào ràng fēng guāxialaile.	墙上的画儿要让风刮下来了。
That magazine hasn't been borrowed (by anyone).	Nà běn zázhì méiyǒu jiào rén jièqu.	那本杂志没有叫人借去。
He was chosen people's representative.	Tā bèi xuǎnzuò rénmín dàibiǎo le.	他被选做人民代表了。
He heard what I said.    He ought not to have heard what I said.	Wǒ shuō de huà tā tīngjianle.  Wǒ shuō de huà ràng tā tīngjian le.	我说的话他听见了。我说的话让他听见了。
The delegation was welcomed by China's people.	Dàibiǎotuán shòudàole zhōngguó rénmín de huānyíng.	代表团受到了中国人民的欢迎。
He's not taller than me.	Tā bù bǐ wǒ gāo.	他不比我高。
He knows more about the school's situation than I do.	Tā bǐ wǒ liǎojiě xuéxiào de qíngkuàng.	他比我了解学校的情况。
His Chinese is much more fluent than mine.	Tā shuō zhōngwén bǐ wǒ liúlì de duō.	他说中文比我流利得多。
This book is much shallower than that one.	Zhèběn shū bǐ nàběn shū qiǎn duō le.	这本书比那本书浅多了。
This one is three meters taller than that one.	Zhège bǐ nàge gāo sān mǐ.	这个比那个高三米。
He came a bit earlier than me.	Tā bǐ wǒ zǎo lái yìdiǎnr.	他比我早来一点儿。
I've studied one less lesson than him.	Wǒ bǐ tā shǎo xué yí kè.	我比他少学一课。
He's not as tall as I am.	Tā méiyǒu wǒ gāo.	他没有我高。
He's come up to my height.	Tā yǒu wǒ zhème gāo le.	他有我这么高了。
We've had some achievements, but we have to keep on working hard.	Wǒmen yǒule yìxiē chéngji, dànshi hái yào búduàn nǔlì.	我们有了一些成绩但是还要不断努力。
I observed a lot of schools and moreover visited a commune.	Wǒ cānguānle bù shǎo xuéxiào, hái fǎngwènle yìge gōngshè.	我参观了不少学校，还访问了一个公社。
I went to see a friend and moreover wrote two letters.	Wǒ qù kànle ge péngyou, hái xiěle liǎng fēng xìn.	我去看了个朋友，还写了两封信。
This film was received even better than that one.	Zhège diànyǐng bǐ nàge hái shòu huānyíng.	这个电影比那个还受欢迎。
I attended a conference.	Wǒ cānjiāle zuòtánhuì.	我参加了座谈会。
I visited the laboratory there.	Wǒ cānguānle nàli de shíyànshì.	我参观了那里的实验室。
In addition to writing letters I also read.	Wǒ chúle xiě xìn (yǐwài), hái kàn shū.	我除了写信（以外），还看书。
He also, in addition to me, hasn't seen that film.	Chúle wǒ yǐwài, tā méi kànguo nàge diànyǐng.	除了我以外，他也没看过那个电影。
Except for him, there's no one else left in the dorm.	Chúle tā yǐwài, sùshè méiyǒu biéde rén le.	除了他以外，宿舍没有别的人了。
Other than two classmates who got sick and couldn't come, everyone came.	Chúle liǎngge tóngxué bìngle bù néng lái (yǐwài), dàjiā dōu láile.	除了两个同学病了不能来（以外），大家都来了。
After graduation he went right to work.	Bìyè yǐhòu, tā jiù qù gōngzuò le.	毕业以后，他就去工作了。
As soon as I got to Beijing I wrote you a letter.	Wǒ dàole běijīng jiù gěi nǐ xiě xìn.	我到了北京就给你写信。
If you're not going out, lend me your bike to ride a bit.	Nǐ bù chūqu jiù bǎ zìxíngchē jiè wǒ qí yíxiàr.	你不出去就把自行车借我骑一下儿。
I've only seen that movie once. (two forms of "only")	Nàge diànyǐng wǒ jiù/zhǐ kànguo yícì.	那个电影我就/只看过一次。
I'm thinking to go again.	Wǒ hái xiǎng zài qù yícì.	我还想再去一次。
Attending the conference were both students and teachers.	Cānjiā zuòtánhuì de, jì yǒu xuéshēng, yòu yǒu jiàoshī.	参观座谈会的，既有学生，又有教师。
Their dorm was both clean and neat.	Tāmen de sùshè jì gānjing, yòu zhěngqí.	他们的宿舍既干净，又整齐。
At the factory, not only the workers labor, but the cadres take part too.	Zài gōngchǎng búdàn gōngrén láodòng, gànbu yě cānjiā láodòng.	在工厂不但工人劳动，干部也参加劳动。
I've not only seen Tian An Men in photos, I've been there.	Tiānānmén wǒ búdàn zài zhàopiànshang kànguo, érqiě hái qùguo.	天安门我不但在照片上看过，而且还去过。
He not only helps me study, he also looks out for me in general.	Tā búdàn bāngzhu wǒ xuéxí, érqiě hái guānxīn wǒ de shēnghuó.	他不但帮助我学习，而且还关心我的生活。
We can not only read these characters, we can write them.	Zhèxiē hànzi wǒmen búdàn huì niàn, érqiě huì xiě.	这些汉字我们不但会念，而且会写。
We had a conference with them.	Wǒmen gēn tāmen jìnxíngle zuòtán.	我们跟他们进行了座谈。
We found out that quite a few students used to be workers.	Liǎojiědào bùshǎo xuéshēng běnlái shi gōngrén.	了解到不少学生本来是工人。
He used to be a PLA member.	Tā běnlái shi jiěfàngjūn.	他本来是解放军。
This university also runs several factories.	Zhège dàxué hái bàn yìxiē gōngchǎng.	这个大学还办一些工厂。
In addition to studying, students also do practical work and take part in labor in the factory.	Xuéshēng chúle xuéxí yǐwài, hái zài gōngchǎng shíjiàn hé cānjiā láodòng.	学生除了学习以外，还在工厂实践和参加劳动。
It helps them resolve questions about combining theory and practice.	Bāngzhu tāmen jiějué lǐlùn hé shíjiàn jiéhé de wèntí.	帮助他们解决理论和实践结合的问题。
It can both help him resolve questions and also produce new products.	Jì néng bāngzhu tā jiějué wèntí, yòu néng shēngchǎn xīn chǎnpǐn.	既能帮助他解决问题，又能生产新产品。
Under the direction of a worker, he assembles a car.	Zài gōngrén de zhǐdǎo xià, tā zhuāngpèi yíliàng qìchē.	在工人的指导下，他装配一辆汽车。
He's in the assembly shop of the car factory.	Tā zài qìchē zhìzàochǎng de zhuāngpèi chējiānli.	他在汽车制造厂的装配车间里。
Surrounding a machine they're having a heated discussion.	Tāmen wéizhe yìtái jīqi rèliè de tǎolùn.	他们围着一台机器热烈地讨论。
That machine was researched and designed by students.	Zhètái jīqi shi xuéshēng yánjiū, shèjì de.	这台机器是学生研究，设计的。
They're summing up their experience.	Tāmen zhèngzài zǒngjié jīngyàn.	他们正在总结经验。
You've served as a teacher for many years, right?	Nǐ dāng lǎoshī yǐjīng hěn duō niánle ba?	你当老师已经很多年了吧？
In many respects, they are my teachers.	Zài hěn duō fāngmiàn tāmen shì wǒ de lǎoshī.	在很多方面他们是我的老师。
What he said left a deep impression on us.	Tā de huà gěi wǒmen líuxiàle shēnkè de yìnxiàng.	他的话给我们留下了深刻的印象。
When the visit was finished, they asked us to leave our opinions.	Cānguān jiéshùle, tāmen qǐng wǒmen bǎ yìjiàn liúxialai.	参观结束了，他们请我们把意见留下来。
Hope you attain even greater achievements.	Zhù nǐ qǔdé gèng dà de chéngji.	祝你取得更大的成绩。
When it turned 10, he was still working.	Shídiǎnle, tā hái zài gōngzuò.	十点了，他还在工作。
I bought a book and, in addition, a map.	Wo mǎile yìběn shū, hái mǎile yìzhāng dìtú.	我买了一本书，还买了一张地图。
The ones who went to see the movie included students and, in addition, teachers.	Qù kàn diànyǐng de, yǒu xuéshēng, hái yǒu lǎoshī.	去看电影的，有学生，还有老师。
His are even neater than yours. (two ways)	Tāde bǐ nǐde (hái|gèng) zhěngqí.	他的比你的（还｜更）整齐。
He's not home except in the evening.	Tā chúle wǎnshang yǐwài, biéde shíhou dōu bú zài jiā.	他除了晚上以外，别的时候都不在家。
He's at home in the afternoon as well as in the evening.	Tā chúle wǎnshang yǐwài, xiàwǔ yě zài jiā.	他除了晚上以外，下午也在家。
Wait a sec, I'll be right there.	Nǐ děng yíhuìr, wǒ jiù lái.	你等一会儿，我就来。
It's just about to rain, don't go out.	Jiùyào xiàyǔle, nǐ búyào chūqule.	就要下雨了，你不要出去了。
As soon as he got back to the dorm he went to sleep.	Tā huídào sùshè jiù shuìle.	他回到宿舍就睡了。
If it rains, we won't go out.	Xiàyǔ jiù bù chūqu.	下雨就不出去。
If you didn't understand, I'll explain it again.	Bù dǒng, wǒ jiù gěi nǐ zài jiǎng yíbiàn.	不懂，我就给你再讲一遍。
He felt a bit tired, so he sat down to rest.	Tā juéde yǒudiǎnr lèi, jiù zuòxialai xiūxile.	他觉得有点儿累，就坐下来休息了。
We're going to see a commune and we'll be back in half a day.	Wǒmen qù cānguān gōngshè, bàntiān jiù kěyi huílai.	我们去参观公社，半天就可以回来。
It's already two-and-a-half months since he left the capital.	Tā líkāi shǒudū yǐjīng liǎnggebàn yuè le.	他离开首都已经两个半月了。
He worked in the countryside for a year and a half.	Tā zài nóngcūn láodòngle yìniánbàn.	他在农村劳动了一年半。
I only did half the exercises, I still have to go on with them in the evening.	Liànxí wǒ gāng zuòle yíbànr, wǎnshàng hái yào jiēzhe zuò.	练习我刚作了一半儿，晚上还要接着作。
The first half is pretty easy, the second half is a bit hard.	Qián yíbànr bǐjiào róngyi, hòu yíbànr yǒu yìdiǎnr nán.	前一半儿比较容易，后一半儿有一点儿难。
Our whole family loves the collective.	Wǒmen quánjiā shéi dōu rèaì jítǐ.	我们全家都热爱集体。
This kind of dictionary is available at any bookstore.	Zhè zhǒng zìdiǎn, nǎge shūdiàn dōu néng mǎidào.	这种字典哪个书店都能买到。
You can come see me tomorrow anytime.	Nǐ míngtiān shénme shíhou lái zhǎo wǒ dōu kěyi.	你明天什么时候来找我都可以。
Wherever there are difficulties, that's where we'll go.	Nǎli yǒu kùnnan, wǒmen jiù dào nǎli qù.	哪里有困难，我们就到哪里去。
Whoever's familiar with the situation in that place, we'll ask to present it.	Shéi liǎojiě nàge dìfang de qíngkuàng, wǒmen jiù qǐng shéi jièshao.	谁了解那个地方的情况，我们就请谁介绍。
I can't analyze this sentence, I'd like to find someone to ask a little (about it).	Zhège jùzi wǒ búhuì fēnxi, xiǎng zhǎo shéi wènwen.	这个句子我不会分析，想找谁问问。
Can you lend me some Chinese book to read for a bit?	Nǐ néngbunéng jiè wǒ yìběn shénme zhōngwén shū kànkan?	你能不能借我一本什么中文书看看？
There was already hardly anyone on the street.	Jiēshang yǐjīng méi duōshǎo rén le.	街上已经没多少人了。
We were coming back very late.	Wǒmen huílai de hěn wǎn.	我们回来得很晚。
It's not yet spring.	Chūntiān hái méi dào ne.	春天还没到呢。
The trees aren't especially green yet.	Shù hái bù zěnme lǜ ne.	树还不怎么绿呢。

We visited an exhibition introducing the history of the commune.	Wǒmen cānguānle yíge jièshào gōngshè lìshǐ de zhǎnlǎn.	我们参观了一个介绍公社历史的展览。
This reservoir was constructed in 1958 after the commune was founded.	Zhège shǔikù shi yījiǔwǔbānián gōngshè chénglì yǐhòu xiūjiàn de.	这个水库是一九五八年公社成立以后修建的。
They relied on the collective's wisdom and strength.	Tāmen yīkào jítǐ de zhìhuì hé lìliang.	他们依靠集体的智慧和力量。
They built it in just over half a year.	Zhǐ yòngle bànnián duō de shíjiān jiù bǎ tā xiūchéngle.	只用了半年多的时间就把它修成了。
The water from this reservoir can irrigate a large part of the land.	Zhège shuǐkù de shuǐ kěyǐ guǎn'gài dà bùfen tǔdì.	这个水库的水可以灌溉大部分土地。
Four years ago this was still a place where nothing could be grown.	Sì nián yǐqián, zhèli hái shi shénme dōu bù zhǎng de dìfang.	四年以前，这里还是什么都不长的地方。
To produce more grain, they moved away the rocks from the valley.	Wèile duō shēngchǎn liángshi, tāmen bānzǒule shāngōu de shítou.	为了多生产粮食，他们搬走了山沟的石头。
To support the construction of socialism, they built terraced fields.	Wèile zhīyuán shèhuìzhǔyì jiànshè, tāmen xiūqǐle tītián.	为了支援社会主义建设，他们修起了梯田。
To foster self reliance, they planted crops.	Wèile fāyáng zìlìgēngshēng, tāmen zhòngshangle zhuāngjia.	为了发扬自力更生，他们种上了庄稼。
They have the spirit of living simply and working hard.	Tāmen yǒu jiānkǔfèndòu de jīngshén.	他们有艰苦奋斗的精神。
They worked bitterly hard through two winters.	Tāmen kǔgànle liǎngge dōngtiān.	他们苦干了两个冬天。
They made it into a high-yielding field in the service of socialism.	Tāmen bǎ tā biànchéngle wèi shèhuìzhǔyì fúwù de fēngchǎn tián.	他们把它变成了为社会主义服务的丰产田。
We didn't even think of the possibility of having the kind of life we have today.	Wǒmen lián xiǎng yě méiyǒu xǐangdào néng yǒu jīntiān zhèyàng de shēnghuó.	我们连想也没有想到能有今天这样的生活。
I feel myself to be still very young.	Wǒ juéde zìjǐ hái hěn niánqīng.	我觉得自己还很年轻。
I still want to live for several decades.	Wǒ hái yào huó jǐshínián ne.	我还要活几十年呢。
Everyone thinks to contribute all his strength.	Shéi dōu xiǎng bǎ zìjǐ suǒyǒu de lìliang gòngxiànchulai.	谁都想把自己所有的力量贡献出来。
A young commune member said: We want to keep on advancing.	Yíwèi qīngnián shèyuán shuō: wǒmen yào búduàn qiánjìn.	一位青年社员说：我们要不断前进。

We fear no difficulties.	Wǒmen shénme kùnnan dōu bú pà.	我们什么困难都不怕。

Whatever time is good for you, that's when I'll go see you.	Nǐ shénme shíhou fāngbian, wǒ jiù shénme shíhou qù zhǎo nǐ.	你什么时候方便，我就什么时候去找你。
Whichever word is appropriate, that's the one to use.	Nǎge cí héshì jiù yòng nǎge cí.	哪个词合适就用哪个词。
However much strength we have, that's how much we contribute.	Wǒmen yǒu duōshǎo lìliang, jiù gòngxiàn duōshǎo lìliang.	我们有多少力量，就贡献多少力量。
I remember who talked to me about this matter.	Wǒ jì de shéi gēn wǒ shuōguo zhèjiàn shì.	我记得谁跟我说过这件事。
Let's go somewhere to have a walk.	Wǒmen dào shénme dìfang qù sànsanbù ba.	我们到什么地方去散散步吧。

It's still raining.	Xiàzhe yǔ ne.	下着雨呢。

Someone's knocking.	Yǒu rén qiāomén.	有人敲门。

Go quick!	Nǐ gǎnkuài qù ba.	你赶快去吧。

I slowly (but continuously) knew more Chinese friends.	Wǒ rènshi de zhōngguó péngyou mànmānr de duōqilai le.	我认识的中国朋友慢慢儿地多起来了。
When they heard the story he told, everyone laughed.	Tīngle tā jiǎng de gùshi, dàjiā dōu xiàoqilai le.	听了他讲的故事，大家都笑起来了。

When the masses moved, they hid all the grain.	Qúnzhòng zhuǎnyí de shíhou, bǎ liángshi dōu cángqilaile.	群众转移的时候，把粮食都藏起来了。

He walked in the lead.	Tā zǒu zài qiántou.	他走在前头。

I'll go right away and borrow records.	Wǒ gǎnkuài jiè chàngpiàn qù ba.	我赶快借唱片去吧。
Please tell him something: I won't be able to return the book till next week.	Qǐng nǐ gàosu tā yìshēng, wǒ xià xīngqī cái néng bǎ shū huán tā.	请你告诉他一声：我下星期才能把书还他。
He said a thing: So long.	Tā shuōle yìshēng: zàijiàn.	他说了一声：再见。
He then biked off.	Tā jiù qí chē zǒule.	他就骑车走了。
When he comes in a while, give me a shout.	Yìhuǐr tā láile, nǐ jiào wǒ yìshēng.	一会儿他来了，你叫我一声。
This commune is right in the vicinity of Beijing.	Zhège rénmín gōngshè jiù zài běijīng fùjìn.	这个人民公社就在北京附近。
There's a post office near our school.	Zánmen xuéxiào fùjìn yǒu yóujú.	咱们学校附近有邮局。
We sometimes go to a nearby construction site to work.	Wǒmen yǒu shíhou dào fùjìn yíge gōngdì qù láodòng.	我们有时候到附近一个工地去劳动。
That scene of frenetic labor caught his attention.	Nà jǐnzhāng de láodòng chǎngmiàn bǎ tā xīyǐnzhùle.	那紧张的劳动场面把他吸引住了。
The brick transporter, pushing a barrow, runs very fast.	Yùn zhuān de tuīzhe xiǎochē fēi pǎo.	运砖的推着小车飞跑。
The bricklayer is also laboring intensely.	Qì zhuān de yě zài jǐnzhāng láodòng.	砌砖的也在紧张劳动。
The megaphone is broadcasting motivational slogans.	Kuòyīnqìli bōsòngzhe gǔdòng de kǒuhào.	扩音器里播送着鼓动的口号。
The megaphone is broadcasting resonant singing.	Kuòyīnqìli bōsòngzhe liáoliàng de gēshēng.	扩音器里播送着嘹亮的歌声。
Bricks will soon be in insufficient supply.	Zhuān kuài gōngbushàng le.	砖快供不上了。
Comrade, step on the gas (i.e. pick up the pace).	Tóngzhì jiāyóu.	同志加油。
He pushes a barrow full to brimming with bricks.	Tā tuīqi mǎnmǎn de yìchē zhuān.	他推起满满的一车砖。
Sweat flows continuously down his face.	Liǎnshang de hàn zhí wàng xià liú.	脸上的汗直往下流。
His clothes were completely wet through.	Tā de yīfu quán shītòule.	他的衣服全湿透了。
His action made them feel moved.	Tā de xíngdòng shǐ tāmen shòu gǎndòng.	他的行动使他们受感动。
The brick pushing comrades packed even more.	Tuī zhuān de tóngzhì zhuāngde gèng duō le.	推砖的同志装得更多了。
Work was finished.	Láodòng jiéshùle.	劳动结束了。
They shook hands with him and declared they wanted to learn from him.	Tāmen hé tā wòshǒu, biǎoshì yào xiàng tā xuéxí.	他们和他握手，表示要向他学习。
This is the factory building we constructed.	Zhè shi wǒmen jiànchéng de chǎngfáng.	这是我们建成的厂房。
There were a lot of brick loaders, they filled the cart in a flash.	Zhuāng zhuān de rén hěn duō, yíxiàzi jiù bǎ chē zhuāngmǎnle.	装砖的人很多，一下子就把车装满了。
Today in a flash it turned cold.	Jīntiān yíxiàzi jiù lěngqilaile.	今天一下子就冷起来了。
There were three days straight of light rain and the crops grew even better.	Yìlián xiàle sān tiān xiǎoyǔ, zhuāngjia zhǎng de gèng hǎo le.	一连下了三天小雨，庄稼长得更好了。
I saw this movie twice in a row.	Zhège diànyǐng, wǒ yìlián kànle liǎng cì.	这个电影，我一连看了两次。
They heard they were going to the park to row boats.	Tāmen tīngshuō yào qù gōngyuán huáchuán.	他们听说要去公园划船。
They happily ran straight along (i.e., without stopping).	Tāmen gāoxìng de zhípǎo.	他们高兴得直跑。
Everyone heard it (the story) smiling straight through.	Dàjiā tīngle dōu zhíxiaò.	大家听了都直笑。
Go have a rest.	Nǐ xiūxi qu ba.	你休息去吧。
Was it to see you that he came?	Tā shi kàn nǐ lái de ma?	他是看你来的吗？
I want to go to the library to take out a book.	Wǒ yào dào túshūguǎn jiè shū qù.	我要到图书馆借书去。
I, downstairs, called him three times till he heard.	Wǒ zài lóuxià jiàole tā sān shēng, tā cái tīngjiàn.	我在楼下叫了他三声，他才听见。
When you head out, give me a shout.	Nǐ zǒu de shíhou, jiào wǒ yìshēng.	你走的时候，叫我一声。
He asks the teacher for a sec if there's a review in the afternoon.	Tā wèn lǎoshi yìshēng xiàwǔ yǒuméiyǒu fǔdaǒ.	他问老师一声下午有没有辅导。
This complex question was settled by the workers with experience.	Zhège fùzá de wèntí bèi yǒu jīngyàn de gōngrén jiějuéle.	这个复杂的问题被有经验的工人解决了。
They were annihilated.	Tāmen bèi xiāomièle.	他们被消灭了。
That world map I bought was borrowed by a friend.	Wǒ mǎi de nàběn shìjiè dìtú jiào péngyou jièqule.	我买的那本世界地图叫朋友借去了。
The laborers are exploited.	Láodòng rénmín shòu bōxuē.	劳动人民受剥削。
The laborers are oppressed.	Láodòng rénmín shòu yāpò.	劳动人民受压迫。
We conducted a long study.	Wǒmen yánjiūle bàntiān.	我们研究了半天。
I don't like to listen to music as much as he does.	Wǒ méiyǒu tā nàyàng xǐhuan tīng yīnyuè.	我没有他那样喜欢听音乐。

Other than Beijing I didn't go anywhere.	Chúle běijīng yǐwài, wǒ nǎr dōu méi qùguo.	除了北京以外，我哪儿都没去过。
In addition to Beijing, I also went to Shanghai.	Chúle běijīng yǐwài, wǒ hái qùguo shànghǎi.	除了北京以外，我还去过上海。
Other than him, none of us studied Chinese before.	Chúle tā yǐwài, wǒmen yǐqián dōu méi xuéguo zhōngwén.	除了他以外，我们以前都没学过中文。
In addition to him, we also haven't studied Chinese before.	Chúle tā yǐwài, wǒmen yǐqián yě méi xuéguo zhōngwén.	除了他以外，我们以前也没学过中文。

He runs into the crop field.	Tā pǎojìn zhuāngjia dìli.	他跑进庄稼地理。

Although it's close, there are a lot of people and traffic.	Jìn dàoshi jìn, kě rén duō chē duō.	近倒是近，可人多车多。
You hit a red light, wait forever without going...on the contrary it's even slower.	Pèngshang hóngdēng, bàntiān guòbuqù, fǎndào gèng màn.	碰上红灯，半天过不去，反倒更慢。
Setting out from school, how about if we head west toward Zhongguancun?	Cóng xuéxiào chūfā, wàng xī bèn zhōngguāncūn zěnme yàng?	从学校出发，往西奔中关村怎么样？
When you get to the Capitol Gymnasium, you turn east.	Dào shǒudū tǐyùguǎn wàng dōng guǎi.	到首都体育馆往东拐。
This is Purple Bamboo Park. (lit. courtyard).	Zhè shi zǐzhúyuàn.	这是紫竹院。
There's Temple of Heaven, Temple of Earth, Temple of the Sun...so many parks.	Yǒu tiāntán, dìtán, rìtán xǔduō gōngyuán ne.	有天坛，地坛，日坛许多公园呢。
Heaven and earth, sun and moon...they're all pairs.	Tiān hé dì, rì hé yuè dōu shi duìzhede.	天和地，日和月都是对着的。
This has to do with the layout of the historic city of Beijing.	Zhè gēn běijīng gǔchéng de bùjú yǒu guānxi.	这跟北京古城的布局有关系。
The old city of Beijing was nearly a perfect square.	Běijīng gǔchéng chàbuduō shi ge zhèng fāngxíng.	北京古城差不多是个正方形。
The Forbidden City is the center.	Gùgōng shi zhōngxīn.	故宫是中心。
The principal roads are all oriented east-west and north-south.	Zhǔyào jiēdào dōu shi dōngxī, nánběi zǒuxiàng.	主要街道都是东西，南北走向。
The principal roads are all perfectly straight.	Zhǔyào jiēdào dōu shi bǐzhíbǐzhí de.	主要街道都是笔直笔直的。
The whole layout lays emphasis on symmetry.	Zhěng ge bùjú jiǎngjiu duìchèn.	整个布局讲究对称。
This was probably characteristic of China's ancient capitals.	Zhè dàgài shi zhōngguó gǔdài jīngchéng de tèdiǎn.	这大概是中国古代京城的特点。
It is said that Xi'an was also like this.	Jùshuō xī'ān yě shi zhè yàng.	据说西安也是这样。
I'm afraid it's more than 30 degrees C.	Kǒngpà yǒu sānshí duō dù.	恐怕有三十多度。
It's a lot hotter than Paris.	Bǐ bālí kě rè duō le.	比巴黎可热多了。
Let's find a spot to cool off.	Zhǎo ge dìfang liángkuài liángkuài ba.	找个地方凉快凉快吧。
Is there a drink place near here?	Fùjìn yǒu lěngyǐndiàn ma?	附近有冷饮店吗？
There's one near the shopping center.	Shāngchǎng fùjìn yǒu.	商场附近有。
I'll also take a half pound of egg rolls.	Zài lái bàn jīn dànjuǎn.	再来半近蛋卷。
They get on their way again.	Tāmen chóngxīn shànglù.	他们重新上路。
On that side of the bridge is the military museum?	Qiáo nàbian shi jūnshì bówùguǎn ma?	桥那边是军事博物馆吗？
Several buildings were built, such as the Military Museum, the Great Hall of the People, and so on.	Gǎole yì xiē jiànzhù, xiàng jūnshì bówùguǎn, rénmín dàhuìtáng děngděng.	搞了一些建筑，象军事博物馆，人民大会堂等等。
All of them are worth visiting.  (i.e. they're important tourist sites)	Dōu zhíde cānguān.	都值得参观。
The Ethnic Cultural Palace is very distinctive.	Mínzú wénhuà gōng hěn yǒu tèsè.	民族文化宫很有特色。
Here they have a Muslim restaurant (i.e. eating place inside the museum).	Zhèlǐ yǒu qīngzhēn cāntīng.	这里有清真餐厅。
Here they have finger food.	Zhèlǐ yǒu zhuā shípǐn.	这里有抓食品。
Here they have roasted foods.	Zhèlǐ yǒu kǎo shípǐn.	这里有烤食品。
Here they have instant-boiled foods.	Zhèlǐ yǒu shuàn shípǐn.	这里有涮食品。
They have special local cuisines.	Yǒu dútè fēngwèi.	有独特风味。
On our way back, how about coming here for a good meal?	Wǒmen huílái shí, dào zhèr měicān yídùn zěnmeyàng?	我们回来时，到这儿美餐一顿怎么样？
I'm just afraid it's too late.	Zhǐ pà tài wǎn le.	只怕太晚了。
It's not too late, they don't close till 9.	Bù wǎn, jiǔdiǎn cái guānmén ne.	不晚，九点才关门呢。

Earning money is one of my goals in this job, but it's not the only goal.	Zhèngqián shi wǒde gōngzuò mùbiāo zhīyī, dàn búshì wéiyī de mùbiāo.	挣钱是我的工作目标之一，但不是唯一的目标。
I hope to realize this goal.	Zhège mùbiāo wǒ xīwàng shíxiàn.	这个目标我希望实现。
My main goal is weight loss.	Wǒ zhǔyào de mùdì jiùshi jiǎnféi.	我主要的目的就是减肥。
My goal is to speak Chinese fluently in the next two years.	Wǒde mùbiāo shi liǎngnián nèi shuō liúlì de zhōngwén.	我的目标是两年内说流利的中文。
My listening ability and grammar is okay. 	Wǒde tīnglì hé yǔfǎ hái kěyǐ.	我的听力和语法还可以。
My vocabulary is limited. 	Wǒde cíhuìliàng yǒuxiàn.	我的词汇量有限。
For example, after an e-mail has been sent, there's no undo.	Lìrú, diànzǐyóujiàn fāsòng yǐhòu jiù bù cúnzài chèxiāo le.	例如，电子邮件发送以后就不存在撤销了。

That dictionary is especially good.  Even if it's expensive, I still want to buy it.	Nàběn zìdiǎn tèbié hǎo.  Jiùshi hěn guì wǒ hái yào mǎi.	那本字典特别好。就是很贵我还要买。
As long as we work hard together, we'll certainly succeed.	Zhǐyào wǒmen yìqǐ nǔlì hézuò, wǒmen yídìng huì chénggōng.	只要我们一起努力合作，我们一定会成功。
Unless you're a millionaire, you'd better not go look at the houses over there.	Chúfēi nǐ shi bǎiwàn fùwēng, yàoburán nǐ zuì hǎo bié qù kàn nàbian de fángzi.	除非你是百万富翁，要不然你最好别去看那边的房子。
Hurry up, otherwise we'll be late for class.	Kuài yìdiǎn ba, yàoburán shàngkè yòu yào chídào le.	快一点吧，要不然上课又要迟到了。
My car is broken, otherwise I wouldn't miss work.	Wǒde qìchē huài le, yàoburán wǒ búhuì bù lái shàngbān.	我的汽车坏了，要不然我不会不来上班。
It's a good thing I'm healthy, otherwise I'd certainly get sick.	Xìngkuī wǒde shēntǐ hǎo, bùrán yídìng huì shēngbìng.	幸亏我的身体好，不然一定会生病。
Lucky I brought some extra money, otherwise we wouldn't be able to get back.	Xìngkuī wǒ duō dàile diǎn qián, fǒuzé wǒmen jiù huíbuqù le.	幸亏我多带了点钱，否则我们就回不去了。
