I eat bread and butter.	Wǒ chī miànbāo hé huángyóu.	我吃面包和黄油。
I eat a hard-boiled egg and fruit.	Wǒ chī zhǔdàn hé shuǐguǒ.	我吃煮蛋和水果。
I like roast duck.	Wǒ chī kǎoyā.	我吃烤鸭。
I don't have a knife or fork.	Dāozi hé chāzi wǒ méiyǒu.	刀子和叉子我没有。
I don't have a glass or a spoon.	Bēizi hé sháozi wǒ méiyǒu.	杯子和勺子我没有。
Which way?  Keep going straight.	Zěnme zǒu?  Wàng qián zǒu.	怎么走？往前走。
Turn right when you get to the traffic light up ahead.	Dào qiánbian hónglǜdēng, wàng yòu guǎi.	到前边红绿灯，往右拐。
Is it far from here?	Lí zhèr yuǎn ma?	离这儿远吗？
How many minutes to get there?	Zǒu duōshǎo fēn zhōng?	走多少分钟？
I put on a coat.	Wǒ chuānshàngle wàitào.	我穿上了外套。
Excuse me, I'm getting off here. (i.e. let me pass)	Láojiàle, wǒ xiàchē.	劳驾了，我下车。
He's my driver.	Tā shi wǒde sījī.	他是我的司机。
Do you have any change? (i.e. coins)	Nǐ yǒu méiyǒu língqián?	你有没有零钱？
How do you want it? (at the barber)	Lǐ shénme yàngde?	理什么样的？
Same as before.  (at the barber)	Zhào yuán yàng lǐ.	照原样理。
Just trim it up a little.  (at the barber)	Zhǐ jiǎn duǎn diǎn jiù kěyǐ le.	只剪短点就可以了。
The barber gave him a shave and a haircut.	Lǐfàshī gěi tā xiūmiàn lǐfà.	理发师给他修面理发。
Please trim my moustache a bit.	Qǐng gěi xiū yíxià húzi.	请给修一下胡子。
I have a headache, a cough and I feel weak.	Tóuténg, késou, juéde quán shēn méi jìnr.	头疼，咳嗽，觉得全身没劲儿。
Are you running a fever?	Fābufā shāo?	发不发烧？
Let me take your temperature.	Nǐ liángyiliáng tǐwēn ba.	你量一量体温吧。
Open your mouth.	Zhāngkāi zǔi.	张开嘴。
Open up your coat.  (i.e. unbutton or unzip it)	Jiěkāi shàngyī.	解开上衣。
You caught a cold.	Nǐ gǎnmào le.	你感冒了。
What have you got?  Nothing serious.  (i.e. a cold)	Shénme bìng?  Bù yàojǐn.	什么病？不要紧。
Do you feel feverish?	Nǐ juéde fāshāo ma?	你觉得发烧吗？
My blood pressure's a bit low.	Wǒ xuèyā piān dī.	我血压偏低。
What kind of person is best suited to become a nurse?	Nǎ zhǒng rén zuì héshì zuò hùshi?	哪种人最合适做护士？
The doctor took an X-ray of the patient's chest.	Yīshēng gěi bìngrén de xiōngbù pāile yì zhāng X guāng piàn.	医生给病人的胸部拍了一张X光片。
Acupuncture can work marvels.	Zhēnjiǔ néng chuàngzào qíjì.	针灸能创造奇迹。
Take the medicine three times a day.	Chīyào yìtiān sāncì.	吃药一天三次。
Will you please iron this suit of mine?	Qǐng nǐ bǎ wǒ zhè tào yīfu gěi yùn yíxià.	请把我这套衣服给熨一下。
When can I pick it up? (i.e. the clothes I left to be cleaned)	Shénme shíhou lái qǔ?	什么时候来取？
Please give me a receipt.	Qǐng gěi wǒ kāi fāpiào.	请给我开发票。
Pay now? (i.e. rather than afterward)	Xiànzài shōu qián ma?	现在收钱吗？
Pay when you pick it up.	Qǔ de shíhou shōufèi.	取的时候收费。
What do you want cleaned?  I'm not cleaning anything.	Nǐ yào xǐ shénme?  Bù xǐ shénme.	你要洗什么？不洗什么。
Do you mind?	Nǐ jièyì ma?	你介意吗？
An idea formed in her mind. 	Tā nǎozilǐ shēngchéngle yíge zhǔyì.	她脑子里生成了一个主意。 
I would rather you tell me the truth.	Wǒ nìngyuàn tīng nǐ shuō shíhuà.	我宁愿听你说实话。
I would rather eat noodles than rice.	Wǒ nìngyuàn chī miàntiáo yě bù yào chī mǐfàn.	我宁愿吃面条也不要吃米饭。
Don't tell me you'd rather be hungry.	Nándào nǐ nìngyuàn è zhe?	难道你宁愿饿着？
Why do you prefer Shanghai?	Nǐ wèishěnme bǐjiào xǐhuān shànghǎi?	你为什么比较喜欢上海？
Generally speaking, this job is not too difficult.	Zǒngdeláishuō, zhège gōngzuò búshì hěn nán.	总的来说，这个工作不是很难。
The flavor of northerners’ food is generally a little stronger.	Běifāngrén de kǒuwèi yìbān bǐjiào zhòng.	北方人的口味一般比较重。
Generally speaking, in the north it's mainly bread and noodles.	Yìbānláishuō, běifāngrén yǐ miànshí wéizhǔ.	一般来说，北方人以面食为主。
Generally it can be delivered within two to three hours. 	Yìbān liǎng sān ge xiǎoshí jiù kěyǐ sòngdào.	一般两三个小时就可以送到。
Most people who come to my store are return customers.	Lái wǒ zhè diànlǐ de dàbùfēn dōu shi huítóukè.	来我这店里的大部分都是回头客。
I'm so excited!	Tài jīdòngle!	太激动了！
Everyone was very excited to see him win.	Kàndào tā yíngle, dàjiā dōu hěn jīdòng.	看到他赢了，大家都很激动。
How come you don't look at all excited?	Nǐ zěnme kànqǐlái yìdiǎn yě bù xīngfèn a?	你怎么看起来一点也不兴奋啊？
I prefer brown rice.	Wǒ bǐjiào xǐhuān chī cāomǐfàn.	我比较喜欢吃糙米饭。
You're right.  Go on.	Nǐ shuōde duì.  Jìxù ba.	你说的对，继续吧。
You're right. (3 ways)	Nǐ shuō de duì, méicuò, yěshì	你说的对，没错，也是
I'm doing it for your own good.	Wǒ shì wèi nǐ hǎo.	我是为你好。
He's on the road to the airport.	Tā zài qù jīchǎng de lùshang.	他在去机场的路上。
The suit needs to be dry cleaned.	Xīfú yào gānxǐ.	西服要干洗。
You are really amazing. You can even knit a sweater.	Nǐ zhēn lìhai, lián máoyī dōu huì zhī.	你真厉害，连毛衣都会织。
I'll put some clean sheets on the bed for you.	Wǒ jiānggěi nǐ pūshang gānjìng de chuángdān.	我将给你铺上干净的床单。
No need to fold the blanket.	Búyòng dié bèizi.	不用叠被子。
The exchange rate is 1 to 1.35	Duìhuànlǜ shi yī bǐ yīdiǎnsānshíwǔ.	兑换率是１比1.35。
Buddy, China has nine hundred million peasants.	Dàgē, zhōngguó yǒu jiǔ yì nóngmín.	大哥，中国有九亿农民。
What's the population of the US?  300 million.	Měiguó yǒu duōshǎo rénkǒu?  Sānyì ge rén.	美国有多少人口？3亿个人。
Have a look at the employee handbook.	Nǐ kànkan yuángōng shǒucè.	你看看《员工手册》。
Which books do you have on acupuncture?	Guānyú zhēnjiǔ de shū yǒu nǎxiē?	关于针灸的书有哪些？
You absolutely can't call me an author; I don't deserve it at all.	Qiānwàn bié jiào wǒ zuòjiā, wǒ kě bù gǎndāng.	千万别叫我作家，我可不敢当。
You can search by the title or author's name, or you can search by price.	Nǐ kěyǐ àn shūmíng huò zuòzhě sōusǒu, yě kěyǐ àn jiàgé sōusǒu.	你可以按书名或作者搜索，也可以按价格搜索。
How long does it normally take to get to Tokyo?	Dào dōngjīng yìbān děi jǐ tiān?	到东京一般得几天？
Which kind do you like, you pick.	Nǐ xǐhuān nǎ zhǒng, zìjǐ tiāo ba.	你喜欢哪种，自己挑吧。
I'll weigh it.	Wǒ liángyiliáng.	我量一量。
Have you got a library card with you?	Nǐ dài jièshūzhèng láile ma?	你带借书证来了吗？
If you can't finish reading it by the end of that time, you can come renew it.	Dào shíjiān kànbuwán kěyǐ lái xùjiè.	到时间看不完可以来续借。
I'll take care of that for you.  (librarian renewing a book for a patron)	Wǒ gěi nǐ bàn.	我给你办。
It makes up 1/4 of the world's population.	Zhàn quán shìjiè rénkǒu de sì fēnzhī yī.	占全世界人口的四分之一。
China is a crowded country.	Zhōngguó shi yíge hěn jǐ de guójiā.	中国是一个很挤的国家。
Not only the cities, but also the countryside is crowded.	Búdàn chéngli jǐ, xiāngxià yě hěn jǐ.	不但城里挤，乡下也很挤。
Five people are squeezed into a small room.	Wǔ kǒu rén jǐ zài yì jiān xiǎo wū​zi lǐ.	五口人挤在一间小屋子里。
The traditional idea is: the more kids the better.	Chuántǒng de guānniàn shi: duōzǐduōfú.	传统的观念是：多子多福。
China all along has been an agricultural society.	Zhōngguó yíxiàng shi nóngyè shèhuì.	中国一向是农业社会。
A great amount of manpower is needed to work in the fields.	Xūyào dàliàng de rénlì zài dìlǐ gōngzuò.	需要大量的人力在地理工作。
Previously, there was no social security system.	Cóngqián méiyǒu shèhuì bǎoxiǎn zhìdù.	从前没有社会保险制度。
In old age it was thus necessary to depend on children to live.	Dàole lǎonián jiù děi kào háizi shēnghuó.	到了老年就得靠孩子生活。
This way of thinking was justified.	Zhèzhǒng de guānniàn shi yǒu dàolǐ de.	这种的观念是有道理的。
Over the last several decades, the politics has changed.	Zuìjìn jǐ shí nián lái, zhèngzhì gǎibiàn le.	最近几十年来，政治改变了。
Because of political, economic, societal all these aspects of change...	Yīnwèi zhèngzhì, jīngjì, shèhuì gè fāngmiàn de gǎibiàn...	因为政治，经济，社会各方面的改变...
The common man gradually recognized: It's a serious burden.	Lǎobǎixìng jiànjiàn rènshi dào: shi yíge hěn zhòng de fùdān.	老百姓渐渐认识到：是一个很重的负担。
Overpopulation is precisely one of the main causes.	Rénkǒu tài duō zhèng shi yíge zhǔyào de yuányīn.	人口太多正是一个主要的原因。
The standard of living is low.	Shēnghuó shǔipíng hěn dī.	生活水平很低。
From the 1970s on, the government promoted the one family one child population policy.	Cóng qīshí niándài qǐ, zhèngfǔ tuīxíng yìjiāyígeháizi de rénkǒu zhèngcè.	从七十年代起，政府推行一家一个孩子的人口政策。
The government advocates contraception.	Zhèngfǔ tíchàng bìyùn.	政府提倡避孕。
Abortion is also used to limit population growth.	Hái yòng duòtāi lái kòngzhì rénkǒu de zēngjiā.	还用堕胎来控制人口的增加。
For households with only one child, the government has rewards.	Duì zhǐ yǒu yíge háizi de jiātíng, zhèngfǔ yǒu jiǎnglì.	对只有一个孩子的家庭，政府有奖励。
Arrangements for the child's future education are good.	Duì háizi jiānglái de jiàoyù yǒu hǎo de ānpái.	对孩子将来的教育有好的安排。
If in spite of the governments stipulations you have more children...	Rúguǒ bù ànzhào zhèngfǔ de guīdìng ér duō shēng háizi...	如果不按照政府的规定而多生孩子...
He receives economic punishment.	Tā shòudào jīngjì de zhìcái.	他受到经济的制裁。
He receives public opinion sanctions.	Tā shòudào yúlùn de zhìcái.	他受到舆论的制裁。
It's also not easy for the child to enter a good school.	Háizi yě bù róngyì jìnrù hǎo xuéxiào.	孩子也不容易进入好学校。
The government rigorously carried out this policy.	Zhèngfǔ yángé de zhíxíng le zhège zhèngcè.	政府严格地执行了这个政策。
Chinese people's "boys rule, girls drool" attitude is deeply rooted.	Zhōngguórén zhòngnánqīngnǚ de guānniàn hěn shēn.	中国人重男轻女的观念很深。
This causes promotion of the policy to run into many difficulties.	Zhè shǐ tuīxíng zhèngcè yùdào xǔduō kùnnan.	这使推行政策遇到许多困难。
The population unceasingly increases.	Rénkǒu búduàn de zēngjiā.	人口不断地增加。
It's still a critical problem.	Háishi yíge yánzhòng de wèntí.	还是一个严重的问题。
I can only (read and) understand 60 percent.	Wǒ zhǐ néng kàndǒng bǎi fēnzhī liùshí.	我只能看懂百分之六十。
At this school, what percentage of students choose to study Chinese?	Xuǎn zhōngwén kè de xuéshēng zhàn quánxiào xuéshēng de jǐ fēnzhī jǐ?	选中文课的学生占全校学生的几分之几？
I hate him.	Wǒ hèn tā.	我恨他。
The more windows, the brighter the room.	Chuāngzi yuè duō fángzi yuè liàng.	窗子越多房子越亮。
The more he eats, the fatter he gets.	Tā yuè chī yuè pàng.	他越吃越胖。
Regarding this matter, I have several thoughts.	Duì zhè jiàn shì wǒ yǒu jǐ diǎn yìjiàn.	对这件事我有几点意见。
This has had a big influence on me.	Zhè duì wǒ yǒu hěn dà de yǐngxiǎng.	这对我有很大的影响。
Exercising more is beneficial to your health.	Duō yùndòng duì nǐ de shēntǐ yǒu hǎochu.	多运动对你的身体有好处。
The government is very concerned with economic issues.	Zhèngfǔ duì jīngjì wèntí hěn guānxīn.	政府对经济问题很关心。
What's your view of this policy?	Nǐ duì zhè ge zhèngcè yǒu shénme kànfǎ?	你对这个政策有什么看法？
In my opinion, this policy is extremely inhumane.	Zài wǒ kànlái zhè ge zhèngcè shi fēicháng bù réndào de.	在我看来这个政策是非常不人道的。
What a husband and wife want to do is entirely their own business.	Yíduì fūfù yào zuò shénme wánquán shi tāmen zìjǐ de shì.	一对夫妇要做什么完全是他们自己的事。
The government shouldn't interfere.	Zhèngfǔ bù yīnggāi gānshè.	政府不应该干涉。
Deciding how many children to have is a personal question.	Shēng jǐge háizi shi gèrén wèntí.	生几个孩子是个人问题。
These two questions can't be completely separated.	Zhè liǎngge wèntí shi bùnéng wánquán fēnkāi de.	这两个问题是不能完全分开的。
The US has many states.	Měiguó yǒu hěn duō zhōu.	美国有很多州。
If you don't wear a seat belt then you have to pay a fine.	Bù bǎng ānquándài jiù děi fáqián.	不绑安全带就得罚钱。
To Chinese people this is hard to comprehend.	Zhè zài zhōngguórén kànlái jiù bútài néng lǐjiě le.	这在中国人看来就不太能理解了。
This is for the purpose of personal safety.	Zhè shi wèile gèrén de ānquán.	这是为了个人的安全。
The government has several responsibilities.	Zhèngfǔ yǒu yìxiē zérèn.	政府有一些责任。
The government attends to issues of the common man's safety.	Zhèngfǔ zhàogù dào lǎobǎixìng de ānquán wèntí.	政府照顾到老百姓的安全问题。
This is a fundamental right of every man.	Zhè shi měi ge rén jīběn de quánlì.	这是每个人基本的权利。
The common man simply no longer has personal freedom.	Lǎobǎixìng jiǎnzhí méiyǒu gèrén zìyóu le.	老百姓简直没有个人自由了。
You can't imagine the problems that can be caused by overpopulation.	Nǐ bùnéng xiǎngxiàng rénkǒu tàiduō huì zàochéng shénme wèntí.	你不能想象人口太多会造成什么问题。
In the late 1950s there was a famine.	Yījiǔwǔlíng niándài mòqī nàole yícì jīhuāng.	一九五〇年代末期闹了一次饥荒。
A huge number of people died of starvation.	È sǐ le qiānqiān wànwàn de rén.	俄死了千千万万的人。
On the one hand, this was the result of policy error.	Zhè yìfāngmiàn shi yīnwèi zhèngcèshàng de cuòwu.	这一方面是因为政策上的错误。
On the other hand, overpopulation was also a principal cause.	Lìng yíge fāngmiàn, rénkǒu guòduō yě shi zhǔyào yuányīn.	另一方面，人口过多也是主要原因。
Overpopulation led to a great famine.	Rénkǒu guòduō zàochéngle dà jīhuāng.	人口过多造成了大饥荒。
Rather than letting children be born and then die of hunger, it's better not to let them be born.	Yǔqí ràng háizi shēngxialai, ránhòu è sǐ, bùrú bú ràng tāmen shēng.	与其让孩子生下来，然后饿死，不如不让他们生。
This way on the contrary is much more humane.	Zhèyàng fǎn'ér réndào xiē.	这样反而人道些。
The economy is not developed.	Jīngjì bù fādá.	经济不发达。
You take the underdeveloped economy and speak as if it had to do with the government.	Nǐ bǎ jīngjì bù fādá, shuō chéng shi yīnwèi zhèngfǔ de guānxī.	你把经济不发达，说成是因为政府的关系。
Living conditions fall short.	Shēnghuó tiáojiàn tài chà.	生活条件太差。
The population density is much higher than China's.	Rénkǒu mìdù bǐ zhōngguó gāodeduō.	人口密度比中国高得多。
In no way is this necessarily a negative.	Zhè bìng bù yídìng shi ge quēdiǎn.	这并不一定是个缺点。
Sometimes it can become a great strength.	Yǒu shíhou kěyǐ biànchéng yìgǔ dà lìliang.	有时候可以变成一股大力量。
What you're saying makes no sense.	Nǐ de huà shi wánquán méiyǒu dàolǐ.	你的话是完全没有道理。
The real problems are not at all now but in the future.	Zhēnzhèng de wèntí bìng búzài xiànzài érshi zài jiānglái.	真正的问题并不在现在而是在将来。
There may be many more old people than young ones.	Lǎonián rén huì bǐ niánqīng rén duōdeduō le.	老年人会比年轻人多得多了。
At the present, many families have an only child.	Mùqián xǔduō jiātíng yǒu dúshēngzǐnǚ.	目前许多家庭有独生子女。
They are all at risk of being spoiled. (e.g. today's only children)	Dōu yǒu bèi guànhuài de kěnéng.	都有被惯坏的可能。
The grandparents' attention is all focused on this child.	Zǔfùmǔ de zhùyìlì dōu jízhōng zhège háizi shēn shàng.	祖父母的注意力都集中这个孩子身上。
Owing to overprotection, a child usually becomes unable to be independent.	Yóuyú guòfèn de bǎohù, háizi wǎngwǎng biànde bùnéng dúlì.	由于过分地保护，孩子往往变得不能独立。
The child usually becomes selfish.	Háizi wǎngwǎng biànde zìsī.	孩子往往变得自私。
There are some issues that were truly not thought of when the policy was established.	Yǒu xiē wèntí quèshí shi zhìdìng zhèngcè de shíhou suǒ méi xiǎngdào de.	有些问题确实是制定政策的时候所没想到的。

Do you mind if I pay in RMB?	Nǐ jièyì wǒ fù rénmínbì ma?	你介意我付人民币吗？
Do you mind if I unload the children onto you this afternoon?	Jīntiān xiàwǔ wǒ bǎ háizi tuōfù gěi nǐ, nǐ bú jièyì ba?	今天下午我把孩子托付给你, 你不介意吧?
In the future, please write to me in Chinese.	Yǐhòu lái xìn qǐng yòng zhōngwén xiě.	以后来信请用中文写。
Why are you applying for this job?	Nǐ wèishénme lái shēnqǐng zhège gōngzuò?	你为什么来申请这个工作？
I like to travel, I'm interested in becoming a tour guide.	Wǒ xǐhuan lǚxíng, wǒ duì dǎoyóu de gōngzuò yǒu xìngqu.	我喜欢旅行，我对导游的工作感兴趣。
In front of others, he criticizes me.	Zài biérén miànqián tā pīpíng wǒ.	在别人面前他批评我。
Studying physics isn't as good as studying psychology.	Yǔqí xué wùlǐ bùrú xué xīnlǐxué.	与其学物理不如学心理学。
His illness not only didn't get better, but on the contrary it worsened.	Tā de bìng búdàn méi hǎo, fǎn'ér gèng lìhài le.	他的病不但没好，反而更厉害了。
Not only didn't he thank me, he cursed me out.	Tā búdàn méi xiè wǒ, fǎn'ér màle wǒ yídùn.	他不但没谢我，反而骂了我一顿。
He didn't come to class because he was sick.	Tā suǒyǐ méilái shàngkè shi yīnwèi tā shēngbìng le.	他所以没来上课是因为他生病了。
Is it because you don't work hard enough that your homework is not good? (2 ways)	Nǐ de gōngkè suǒyǐ bùhǎo shìbushì yīnwèi búgòu yònggōng (de guānxi | yuángù)?	你的功课所以不好是不是因为不够用功（的关系｜缘故）？
It's not a capitalist country, but rather a socialist one.	Búshì zīběnzhǔyì de guójiā, érshi shèhuìzhǔyì de guójiā.	不是资本主义的国家，而是社会主义的国家。
They don't dare to have more children due to fear of governmental punishment.	Tāmen bùgǎn duō shēng háizi shì yóuyú pà zhèngfǔ zhìcái.	他们不敢多生孩子是由于怕政府制裁。
The books I read are all related to history.	Wǒ suǒ kànde shū dōu shi gēn lìshǐ yǒu guānxide.	我所看的书都是跟历史有关系的。
According to what the teacher says, his views are very different.	Zhào lǎoshī suǒ shuōde, tā de kànfǎ hěn bùtóng.	照老师所说的，他的看法很不同。
He gets fat, he becomes a fatso.	Tā biàn pàng, tā biànchéng yíge pàngzi.	他变胖，他变成一个胖子。
Would you mind typing the character for me.  (i.e. can't read the handwriting)	Máfán nín bǎ zì dǎchulai gěi wǒ.	麻烦您把字打出來给我。
Over summer vacation I went on a trip through Asia.	Shǔjià wǒ qùle yítàng yàzhōu.	暑假我去了一趟亚洲。
I've been to both Korea and Thailand.	Hánguó, tàiguó wǒ dōu qùguo.	韩国泰国我都去过。
Ah, so you went to Asia, no wonder I haven't seen you.	Yuánlái nǐ qùle yàzhōu, guàibude méi kàndao nǐ.	原来你去了亚洲，怪不得没看到你。
What all did you do over vacation?	Nǐ zài jiàqīli dōu zuòle xiē shénme ne?	你在假期里都做了些什么呢？
I stayed at school working on my senior thesis. (2 ways)	Wǒ liú/dāi zài xuéxiàoli zhǔnbèi bìyè lùnwén.	我留/待在学校里准备毕业论文。
This semester I have to knuckle down a bit more.	Zhè xuéqī wǒ děi duō yòng diǎnr gōng le.	这学期我得多用点儿功了。
My strongest impressions are of Taiwan.	Wǒ duì táiwān de yìnxiàng zuì shēn.	我对台湾的印象最深。
I discovered that he's actually pretty funny.	Wǒ fāxiàn qíshí tā hěn yōumò.	我发现其实他很幽默。
This is a most interesting phenomenon.	Zhè shi yíge fēicháng yǒuqù de xiànxiàng.	这是一个非常有趣的现象。
Which place left a better impression?	Nǎge dìfang gěi nǐ de yìnxiàng bǐjiào hǎo?	哪个地方给你的印象比较好？
Talk a bit about everyday life.	Nǐ shuōshuo rìcháng shēnghuó ba.	你说说日常生活吧。
Generally speaking, everything's pretty convenient.	Yìbānshuōlái dōu hái fāngbiàn.	一般说来都还方便。
Many places still don't have flush toilets.	Xǔduō dìfang hái méiyǒu chōushǔimǎtǒng.	许多地方还没有抽水马桶。
The flush toilets are often squat toilets.	Chōushǔimǎtǒng cháng shi dūnde.	抽水马桶常是蹲的。
I'm can't get used to using the squat kind. (i.e. toilets)	Dūnde wǒ yòngbuguàn.	蹲的我用不惯。
Actually, the squatting kind are a bit more sanitary than the sitting kind.	Dūnde qíshí bǐ zuòde yào wèishēng yìxiē.	蹲的其实比坐的要卫生一些。
I need to go to the bathroom.	Wǒ yào shàng cèsuǒ.	我要上厕所。
Most residences don't have bathing facilities.	Yìbān zhùjiā shi méiyǒu xǐzǎo shèbèi de.	一般住家是没有洗澡设备的。
This is an even bigger problem.	Zhège wèntí gèng dà.	这个问题更大。
If you want to bathe, you have to go to a public bath house.	Yào xǐzǎo jiù děi qù gōnggòng zǎotáng.	要洗澡就得去公共澡堂。
In these respects, aren't the circumstances a bit better?	Zài zhè xiē fāngmiàn de qíngxíng shìbushì hǎo xiē ne?	在这些方面的情形是不是好些呢？
The thing that most scared me was driving in Taipei.	Ràng wǒ zuì hàipà de shi zài táiběi kāichē.	让我最害怕的是在台北开车。
Traffic in Taipei is even more chaotic than in New York.	Táiběi de jiāotōng qíngkuàng bǐ niǔyuē hái luàn.	台北的交通情况比纽约还乱。
The taxi drivers particularly drive like maniacs.	Yóuqí shi jìchéngchē sījī dōu shi héngchōngzhízhuàng.	尤其是计程车司机都是横冲直撞。
It seems like there are absolutely no traffic rules.	Hǎoxiàng wánquán méiyǒu jiāotōng guīzé de yàngzi.	好象完全没有交通规则的样子。
If there's no policeman watching, the crosswalk has no effect.	Bānmǎxiàn yàoshi méiyǒu jǐngchá kānzhe, jiù qǐbuliǎo zuòyòng.	斑马线要是没有警察看着，就起不了作用。
From what you say, it seems this place is no fun.	Zhào nǐ zhème shuō lái, zhège dìfang hǎoxiàng bùhǎo wánr.	照你这么说来，这个地方好象不好玩儿。
Don't by any means get me wrong.	Nǐ kě qiānwàn bié wùhuì wǒ de yìsi.	你千万别误会我的意思。
You just brought up the topic of Beijing.  (i.e. so let's discuss it)	Gāngcái nǐ tídào běijīng.	刚才你提到北京。
What's distinctive about this city.	Zhège chéngshì yǒu shénme tèsè.	这个城市有什么特色？
This is the site of the capital.	Zhè shi shǒudū de suǒzàidì.	这是首都的所在地。
It's among China's most ancient cities.	Shì zhōngguó zuì gǔlǎo de chéngshì zhīyī.	是中国最古老的城市之一。
You can still see many Ming dynasty buildings.	Hái néng kàndào xǔduō míngcháo de jiànzhù.	还能看到许多明朝的建筑。
Several buildings in the city center have a bit of a European flavor.	Shì zhōngxīn de yìxiē jiànzhù yǒu diǎnr ōuzhōu de fēngwèi.	市中心的一些建筑有点儿欧洲的风味。
It makes people think of the late 19th century.	Shǐ rén xiǎngdào shíjiǔ shìjì mònián.	使人想到十九世纪末年。
The period of the early 20th century imperialist invasions of China is very interesting.	Èrshí shìjì chūnián dìguózhǔyì qīnlǜe zhōngguó de nà duàn rìzi hěn yǒu yìsi.	二十世纪初年帝国主义侵略中国的那段日子很有意思。
This is present day China's most modernized city.	Zhè shi mùqián zhōngguó zuì xiàndàihuà de chéngshì.	这是目前中国最现代化的城市。
It's very westernized.	Hěn xīhuà.	很西化。
It's a lot like Hong Kong.	Gēn xiānggǎng hěn xiàng.	跟香港很象。
Every year it attracts a huge number of tourists.	Měinián néng xīyǐn chéngqiānshàngwàn de guān'guāngkè.	每年能吸引成千上万的观光客。
From what my friends have told me, the policy has changed.	Jù wǒ de péngyǒu gēn wǒ shuō, zhèngcè gǎibiàn le.	据我的朋友跟我说，政策改变了。
Production is quite a number of times higher than before.	Shēngchǎn bǐ yǐqián zēngjiā le hǎo jǐ bèi.	生产比以前增加了好几倍。
The peasants' income has increased.	Nóngmín de shōurù tígāole.	农民的收入提高了。
Life has improved.	Shēnghuó gǎishànle.	生活改善了。
In the city there have gotten to be many more free markets.	Chéngshìlǐ duōle xǔduō zìyóu shìchǎng.	城市里多了许多自由市场。
In the past, there were often shortage conditions.	Cóngqián chángyǒu quēhuò de qíngxíng.	从前常有缺货的情形。
Commodity prices have gone up a lot compared to the past.	Wùjià bǐ cóngqián zhǎngle xǔduō.	物价比从前涨了许多。
I read in the paper that there are also crime problems.	Wǒ kàn bàoshang yě yǒu shèhuì zhì'ān de wèntí.	我看报上也有社会治安的问题。
Does this have something to do with the opening up of economic policies?	Zhè gēn jīngjì zhèngcè kāifàng yǒuméiyǒu guānxi?	这跟经济政策开放有没有关系？
Everyone's lifestyle was about the same.	Dàjiā shēnghuó de fāngshì dàzhì shi yíyàngde.	大家生活的方式大致是一样的。
From hairstyles to clothing, they've all gotten to have a fairly large selection.	Cóng fàxíng dào fúzhuāng, dōu yǒule bǐjiào duō de xuǎnzé.	从发型到服装都有了比较多的选择。
Compared to before, the temptations are greatly increased on all sides.	Gè fāngmiàn de yòuhuò bǐ cóngqián dà de hěn duō le.	各方面的诱惑比从前大得很多了。
Ergo, society's robbery and theft cases are somewhat more numerous than previously.	Yīncǐ shèhuìshang qiǎngjié, tōuqiè de ànzi bǐ cóngqián duō xiē.	因此社会上抢劫，偷窃的案子比从前多些。
Nevertheless, if you compare China and the US, China is still a safe place.	Búguò ná zhōngguó gēn měiguó bǐjiào, zhōngguó hái shì yīge ānquán de dìfang.	不过拿中国跟美国比较，中国还是一个安全的地方。
Politically, is it also more open than previously?	Zài zhèngzhìshang shìbushì yě bǐ cóngqián kāifàng?	在政治上是不是也比从前开放？
Economically, China seems to be taking the capitalist road.	Zài jīngjìshang, zhōngguó hǎoxiàng zài zǒu zīběnzhǔyì de dàolù.	在经济上，中国好象在走资本主义的道路。
China is a communist country.	Zhōngguó shi yíge gòngchǎnzhǔyì de guójiā.	中国是一个共产主义的国家。
Recently it's opened up a bit regarding free speech.	Zuìjìn duì yánlùnzìyóu kāifàngle yìxiē.	最近对言论自由开放了一些。
Within certain limits, the common man can criticize the government.	Lǎobǎixìng kěyǐ zài yídìng de fànwéi nèi pīpíng zhèngfǔ.	老百姓可以在一定的范围内批评政府。
He can bring up some ideas that aren't the same as the government's.	Tā kěyǐ tíchū yìxiē yǔ zhèngfǔ bùtóng de yìjiàn.	他可以提出一些与政府不同的意见。
In the past, this was absolutely not permitted.	Zhè zài cóngqián shi juéduì bù yǔnxǔ de.	这在从前是绝对不允许的。
If you help him, he'll be able to succeed.	Rúguǒ nǐ bāngzhu tā de huà, tā jiù huì chénggōngde.	如果你帮助他的话，他就会成功的。
I looked up and down for my pen without finding it, turns out he took it.	Wǒde bǐ zhǎolái zhǎoqù dōu zhǎobudào, yuánlái shi tā názǒule.	我的笔找来找去都找不到，原来是他拿走了。
Later he came east to study.	Hòulái dào dōngbù lái niànshū.	后来到东部来念书。
I sold it to him.	Wǒ mài gěi tā le.	我卖给他了。
I read that book for three days; I haven't read that book for three days.	Wǒ nàběn shū kànle sān tiān; wǒ sān tiān méi kàn nà běn shū.	我那本书看了三天，我三天没看那本书。
I haven't seen you for a few months.	Jǐge yuè dōu méi kàndào nǐ.	几个月都没看到你。
If I don't eat for three days, I'll definitely starve to death.	Yàoshi wǒ sāntiān bù chīfàn yídìng huì è sǐ.	要是我三天不吃饭一定会饿死。
I haven't called my son in a month.	Wǒ yǒu yíge yuè méi gěi érzi dǎ diànhuà le.	我有一个月没给儿子打电话了。
I don't know of any news.	Xīnwén wǒ dōu bù zhīdào.	新闻我都不知道。
It left a strong impression on me; I have a strong impression of it.	Tā gěi wǒ liúxiale hěn shēn de yìnxiàng, wǒ duì tā de yìnxiàng hěn shēn.	它给我留下了很深的印象，我对它的印象很深。
Unless you're married with kids, you can't apply.	Chúfēi shi jiélehūn érqiě yǒu háizi de rén, biéde rén dōu shi shēnqǐng búdào de.	除非是结了婚而且有孩子的人，别的人都是申请不到的。
Except people with their own kitchen, everyone has to eat in the dining hall.	Chúfēi zìjǐ yǒu chúfáng, měige rén dōu děi zài cāntīng chīfàn.	除非自己有厨房，每个人都得在餐厅吃饭。
I haven't seen you for almost a month.	Kuài yìge yuè méi kàndào nǐ.	快一个月没看到你。
I'm staying home.	Wǒ liú zài jiālǐ.	我留在家里。
Only people with their own kitchens can not eat in the cafeteria.	Chúfēi zìjǐ yǒu chúfáng cái kěyǐ búzài cāntīng chīfàn.	除非自己有厨房才可以不在餐厅吃饭。
Unless the weather's good, I'm not going out.	Chúfēi tiānqì hǎo, wǒ shi bù chūqù de	除非天气好，我是不出去的。
He seems not to have heard me speak.	Tā hǎoxiàng méi tīngjiàn wǒ shuōhuà shìde.	他好象没听见我说话似的。
You seem very familiar with Beijing.	Nǐ hǎoxiàng duì běijīng hěn shúxī.	你好象对北京很熟悉。
You absolutely must drive carefully.	Nǐ qiānwàn děi xiǎoxīn kāichē.	你千万得小心开车。
Don't by any means walk outside late at night.	Nǐ qiānwàn bié zài shēnyè de shíhou zài wàitóu zǒulù.	你千万别在深夜的时候在外头走路。
Don't under any circumstances believe what he says.	Nǐ qiānwàn bié xiāngxìn tā de huà.	你千万别相信他的话。
New York is the location of the United Nations.	Niǔyuē shi liánhéguó de suǒzàidì.	纽约是联合国的所在地。
This is one of my favorite courses.	Zhè ménkè shi wǒ zuì xǐhuān de kè zhīyī.	这门课是我最喜欢的课之一。
This is one of the reasons I came to study at this college.	Zhè shi wǒ dào zhèsuǒ dàxué niànshū de yuányīn zhīyī.	这是我到这所大学念书的原因之一。
He and his mother are much alike.	Tā gēn tāde mǔqin hěn xiàng.	他跟他的母亲很象。
In comparison with high school students, college students have more freedom.	Ná gāozhōng gēn dàxué bǐjiào, dàxué de xuéshēng yǒu bǐjiào duō de zìyóu.	拿高中跟大学比较，大学的学生有比较多的自由。
These two cities have many points in common.	Zhè liǎng ge chéngshì yǒu xǔduō xiāngtóng de dìfang.	这两个城市有许多相同的地方。

If you'd helped him, he would have been able to succeed.	Rúguǒ nǐ bāngle tā de huà, tā yīnggāi zǎojiù chénggōngle.	如果你帮了他的话，他应该早就成功了。
Confucius is China's greatest thinker.	Kǒngzǐ shi zhōngguó zuì wěidà de sīxiǎngjiā.	孔子是中国最伟大的思想家。
He is the founder of Confucianism.	Tā shi rújiāxuéshuō de chuàngshǐrén.	他是儒家学说的创始人。
He was born in 551 BC. (two ways)	Tā shēng zài (xī/gōng)yuánqián wǔwǔyī nián.	他生在(西/公)元前五五一年。
It was also the Spring and Autumn period of Chinese history.	Yě shi zhōngguó lìshǐshang de chūnqiū shídài.	也是中国历史上的春秋时代。
China was divided into many small countries. (at that time)	Zhōngguó fēnlièchéng xǔduō xiǎo guó.	中国分裂成许多小国。
It was not at all a unified country.	Bìng búshì yíge tǒngyī de guójiā.	并不是一个统一的国家。
He was tall of stature.	Tāde gèzi hěn gāo.	他的个子很高。
After becoming an adult, he served as a petty official.	Chéngrén yǐhòu tā zuòguo xiǎo guān.	成人以后他做过小官。
He had to leave Lu and travel in neighboring (small) countries.	Tā zhǐhǎo líkāi lǔguó dào línjìn de xiǎoguó qù lǚxíng.	他只好离开鲁国到邻近小国旅行。
He found a job.	Tā zhǎodàole yífèn gōngzuò.	他找到了一份工作。
His lifelong dream is to realize his own political ideal.	Tā yìshēng de yuànwàng shi shíxiàn tā zìjǐ de zhèngzhì lǐxiǎng.	他一生的愿望是实现他自己的政治理想。
He hopes to realize his ideal through some country's leader.	Tā xīwàng tōngguò yì guó de jūnzhǔ shíxiàn tā de lǐxiǎng.	他希望通过一国的君主实现他的理想。
Among these leaders there weren't any able to appreciate his value.	Zhè xiē jūnzhǔ méiyǒu yíge néng shǎngshí tāde cáinéng.	这些君主没有一个能赏识他的才能。
Deeply disappointed, he returned to his native home. (i.e. the area where he originally lived)	Tā fēicháng shīwàng de huídào jiāxiāng.	他非常失望地回到家乡。
Nevertheless, his ideas became the main current of Chinese philosophy.	Tāde sīxiǎng què chéngle zhōngguó zhéxué de zhǔliú.	他的思想却成了中国哲学的主流。
For over two thousand years, no dynasty's government has failed to receive his influence.	Liǎng qiān duō nián lái méiyǒu yíge cháodài de zhèngfǔ búshòu tā de yǐngxiǎng.	两千年多来没有一个朝代的政府不受他的影响。
Tradition has it that he had more than 3,000 students.	Chuánshuō tā yǒu sānqiānduō xuéshēng.	传说他有三千多学生。
This book, the Analects, is precisely a record of him and his students chatting.	"Lúnyǔ" zhè běn shū jiùshi tā gēn tā xuéshēng tánhuà de jìlù.	＂论语＂这本书就是他跟他学生谈话的记录。
Nearly every educated Chinese person has read/studied this book	Fánshì shòuguo jiàoyù de zhōngguórén chàbuduō dōu dúguo zhè běn shū.	凡是受过教育的中国人差不多都读过这本书。
He teaches people to respect/obey their parents.	Tā jiāo rén xiàoshùn fùmǔ.	他较人孝顺父母。
Jesus says you must love your enemy.	Yēsū shuō yào ài nǐ de dírén.	耶稣说要爱你的敌人。
You turn your right cheek to let him strike that too.	Nǐ bǎ yòuliǎn yě zhuǎnguoqù ràng tā dǎ.	你把右脸也转过去让他打。
He's a practical man.	Tā shi yíge hěn shíjì de rén.	他是一个很实际的人。
He doesn't teach people to go put into practice an impossible teaching.	Tā bù jiāo rén qù shíxíng yíge zuòbudào de jiàoxùn.	他不较人去实行一个做不到的教训。
Regarding politics, Confucious is relatively conservative.	Zài zhèngzhìshang, kǒngzǐ shi bǐjiào bǎoshǒu de.	在政治上孔子是比较保守的。
He hopes to preserve the old system.	Tā xīwàng wéichí jiù zhìdù.	他希望维持旧制度。
He hopes to preserve the old social order.	Tā xīwàng wéichí jiù zhìxù.	他希望维持旧秩序。
For those with authority and power this was often advantageous.	Zhè duì yǒu quán yǒu shì de rén wǎngwǎng shi yǒu lì de.	这对有权有势的人往往是有利的。
He was a great learned scholar.	Tā shi yíge hěn yǒu xuéwèn de dà xuézhě.	他是一个很有学问的大学者。
He was extremely versed in the ancient (Chinese) classics.	Tā duì gǔdài de jīngdiǎn fēicháng shúxī.	他对古代的经典非常熟悉。
He may have done some (scholarly) compilation/systematization work.	Tā kěnéng zuòguo yìxiē zhěnglǐ de gōngzuò.	他可能做过一些整理的工作。
Owing to the then government's promotion of Confucianism...	Yóuyú dāngshí zhèngfǔ duì rújiāxuéshuō de tíchàng...	由于当时政府对儒家学说的提倡...
From the Han dynasty on it came to represent Chinese academic ideology.	Dàole hàncháo yǐhòu chéngle zhōngguó xuéshù sīxiǎng de dàibiǎo.	到了汉朝以后成了中国学术思想的代表。
Since I had no money I had no choice but not to go.	Yīnwèi méiyǒu qián zhǐhǎo bú qù le.	因为没有钱只好不去了。
Since there aren't any other rooms, he has to live here.	Yīnwèi méiyǒu biéde fángzi, tā zhǐhǎo zhùle.	因为没有别的房子，他只好住了。
Anyone who's studied Chinese knows the grammar is hard.	Fánshì xuéguo zhōngwén de rén, dōu zhīdào zhōngwén yǔfǎ hěn nán.	凡是学过中文的人，都知道中文语法很难。
This plan is of no benefit to me.	Zhège jìhuà duì wǒ méiyǒu lì.	这个计划对我没有利。
Will taking this course help me in the future finding a job?	Shàng zhè mén kè duì jiānglái zhǎo gōngzuò yǒu méiyǒu lì?	上这门课对将来找工作有没有利？
School has already been going for a week.	Kāi xué yǐjīng yíge xīngqi le.	开学已经一个星期了。
This semester I'm taking four courses.	Zhège xuéqī wǒ xuǎnle sì mén kè.	这个学期我选了四门课。
At this point I still haven't decided on a major.	Dào xiànzài wǒ hái méiyǒu juédìng zhuānyè shi shénme.	到现在还没有决定专业是什么。
Maybe from these courses I can figure out what my interests are.	Huòxǔ kěyǐ cóng zhè xiē kèlǐ fāxiàn zìjǐ de xìngqu.	或许可以从这些课里发现自己的兴趣。
I've liked science since I was little.	Wǒ cóng xiǎo xǐhuān kēxué.	我从小喜欢科学。
This course is quite hard.  (i.e. takes a lot of time and effort)	Zhè mén kè xiāngdāng zhòng.	这门课相当重。
In particular, in the chemistry course the professor is very tough.	Yóuqí shi huàxué kè, jiàoshòu hěn yán.	尤其是化学课，教授很严。
I'm doing a lab.	Wǒ zài zuò shíyàn.	我在做实验。
We often have to write reports.	Wǒmen děi jīngcháng xiě bàogào.	我们得经常写报告。
My roommate is also a sophomore.	Wǒ de tóngwū yě shi yíge èrniánjí de xuéshēng.	我的同屋也是一个二年级的学生。
Often calls are still coming in the middle of the night.	Chángcháng bànyè hái yǒu diànhuà lái.	常常半夜还有电话来。
I've spent $100 just on books for physics class.	Guāngshì wùlǐ kè de shū jiù huāle yī bǎi kuài qián.	光是物理课的书就花了一百块钱。
When you write back, ask dad to send another check for me.	Huíxìn de shíhou qǐng bàba zài jì zhāng zhīpiào gěi wǒ.	回信的时候请爸爸再奇张支票给我。
His father is especially tall.	Tā fùqin yóuqí gāo.	他父亲尤其高。
I hate doing housework, especially washing dishes.	Wǒ tǎoyàn zuò jiāshì, yóuqí shi xǐwǎn.	我讨厌做家事，尤其是洗碗。
Wherever you live is fine.	Nǐ zài nǎr zhù dōu xíng.	你在哪儿住都行。
No matter how expensive the books are, I can afford them.	Duōme guì de shū wǒ dōu mǎideqǐ.	多么贵的书我都买的起。
No matter how I do it he's not happy.	Wǒ zěnme zuò tā dōu bù gāoxing.	我怎么做他都不高兴。
Everyone wants to go except him.	Shéi dōu yào qù, jiùshi tā bù xiǎng qù.	谁都要去就是他不想去。
I'm free anytime, just Wednesday I'm not.	Wǒ shénme shíhòu dōu yǒu kòng, jiùshi xīngqī sān méiyǒu kòng.	我什么时候都有空，就是星期三没有空。
Everything about this book is good, it's just too expensive.	Zhè běn shū shénme dōu hǎo, jiùshi tài guì.	这本书什么都好，就是太贵。
He still hasn't graduated.	Tā hái méi bìyè ne.	他还没毕业呢。

Just preparing for Chinese class he spent three hours.	Guāngshi yùbèi zhōngwénkè tā jiù huāle sānge zhōngtóu.	光是预备中文课他就花了三个钟头。
Just to live in the dormitory is five thousand dollars. (imagine the cost of the rest!)	Guāngshi zhù zài sùshè jiù yào wǔqiān kuài qián.	光是住在宿舍就要五千块钱。

When you were in elementary school you hated history most of all.	Nǐ zài xiǎoxué de shíhou zuì tǎoyàn lìshǐ kè.	你在小学的时候最讨厌历史课。
As a result, they don't do well in those subjects. (i.e. those we've been discussing)	Jiéguǒ kè xuébuhǎo.	结果课学不好。

I earn a little pocket money.	Wǒ zhuàn yìxiē língyòngqián.	我赚一些零用钱。

Does knowing Chinese help in getting a job?	Huì shuō zhōngwén duì zhǎo gōngzuò yǒu méiyǒu hǎochu?	会说中文对找工作有没有好处？

He even controls the color of the clothing I wear.	Tā lián wǒ chuān shénme yánsè de yīfu dōu guǎn.	他连我穿什么颜色的衣服都管。
The Grand Canal is the greatest feat of engineering in Chinese history.	Dàyùnhé shi zhōngguó lìshǐshang zuì wěidà de gōngchéng.	大运河是中国历史上最伟大的工程。
Its full length is approximately 6,700 kilometers.	Quáncháng dàyuē yǒu liùqiān qībǎi gōnglǐ.	全长大约有六千七百公里。
According to the usual way of putting it, the Great Wall was built by Qin ShiHuang.	Zhào yìbān de shuōfǎ, chángchéng shi qín shǐhuáng jiànde.	照一般的说法，长城是秦始皇建的。
The greater part was built in the Ming dynasty.	Dàduō shi míngdài xiūzhùde.	大多是明代修筑的。
It was originally to prevent the north's enemies from invading southward.	Yuánlái shi wèile fángzhǐ běifāng de dírén xiàng nánbiān qīnlǜe.	原来是为了防止北方的敌人向南边侵略。
In the final analysis, did the Great Wall have this effect?	Chángchéng dàodǐ qǐle zhège zuòyòng méiyǒu ne?	长城到底起了这个作用没有呢？
From the Qin and Han straight through to Ming and Qing, not one dynasty escaped trouble in the north.	Cóng qín, hàn yìzhí dào míng, qīng, méiyǒu yíge cháodài táoguo běifāng de wàihuàn.	从秦，汉一直到明，清，没有一个朝代逃过北方的外患。
The whole country perished in the hands of the Mongolians.	Zhěngge guójiā dōu wáng zài ménggǔrén de shǒulǐ le.	整个国家都亡在蒙古人的手里了。
I consider that the significance of the Great Wall in national defense is miniscule.	Wǒ rènwéi chángchéng zài guófángshàng de yìyì shi jíxiǎo de.	我认为长城在国防上的意义是极小的。
On the contrary, it restricted the development of Chinese people northward.	Fǎnér, xiànzhì le zhōngguórén wàng běifāng de fāzhǎn.	反而限制了中国人往北方的发展。
Straight through to this day, to the north of the Great Wall is still way underdeveloped compared to the area to the south.	Yìzhí dào jīntiān, chángchéng yǐběi hái bǐ chángchéng yǐnán luòhòu de duō.	一直到今天，长城以北还比长城以南落后得多。
In addition to geographical reasons, the Great Wall was certainly also a factor.	Chúle dìlǐshàng de yuángù, chángchéng yě yǒu yídìng de yǐngxiǎng.	除了地理上的缘故，长城也有一定的影响。
It's certainly something unexpected.	Shízài shi yíjiàn xiǎngbudào de shì.	实在是一件想不到的事。
The Great Wall is the result of the blood and sweat of thousands upon thousands of ordinary people.	Chángchéng shi qiānqiānwànwàn de lǎobǎixìng liúxiěliúhàn de jiéguǒ.	长城是千千万万的老百姓流血流汗的结果。
The Great Canal is a man-made river.	Dàyùnhé shi yìtiáo réngōng kāijiànde héliú.	大运河是一条人工开建的河流。
The Great Canal joins the two cities of Beijing and Hangzhou.	Dàyùnhé bǎ běijīng hé hángzhōu zhè liǎngge chéngshì lián zài yìqǐ.	大运河把北京和杭州这两个城市连在一起。
This is our great achievement in transportation and irrigation engineering.	Zhè shi wǒmen zài jiāotōng hé shuǐlì liǎng xiàng gōngchéngshàng de wěidà chéngjiù.	这是我们在交通和水利两项工程上的伟大成就。
From the beginning of the Sui dynasty straight through to the middle of the Qing dynasty...	Cóng suícháo kāishǐ, yìzhí dào qīngcháo de zhōngqī...	从隋朝开始，一直到清朝的中期...
China's north-south cultural exchange all depended on the Great Canal.	Zhōngguó nánběi de wénhuà de jiāoliú quán kào dàyùnhé.	中国南北的文化的交流全靠大运河。
They started to build railways.	Tāmen kāishǐ jiànshè tiělù.	他们开始建设铁路。
The Great Canal's importance declined day by day.	Dàyùnhé de dìwèi yìtiān bùrú yìtiān le.	大运河的地位一天不如一天了。
Whether in terms of national defense or culture, its contributions are large.	Wúlùn zài guófángshàng, háishi wénhuàshàng, tā de gòngxiàn hěn dà.	无论在国防上，还是文化上，它的贡献很大。

He has no skills, what would he live on?	Tā méiyǒu jìnéng, yòng shénme lái wéichí shēnghuó?	他没有技能，用什么来维持生活？
He alway says our ideas are out-of-date.	Tā zǒng shuō wǒmen de guānniàn luòwǔ le.	他总说我们的观念落伍了。
So long as a boy and girl love each other, they can live together.	Nánnǚ zhǐyào xiāng'ài jiù kěyǐ shēnghuó zài yìqǐ.	男女只要相爱就可以生活在一起。
What's the difference whether or not they get married?	Jiéhūn bù jiéhūn yòu yǒu shénme guānxi ne?	结婚不结婚又有什么关系呢？
From 1979 on, I've lived continuously in the US.	Zìcóng 1979 nián yǐhòu, wǒ yìzhí zhùzài měiguó.	自从1979年我一直住在美国。
Ever since I learned Chinese, I've met more and more Chinese people.	Wǒ zìcóng xuéle zhōngwén yǐhòu, rènshi de zhōngguórén yuèláiyuèduō le.	我自从学了中文以后，认识的中国人越来越多了。
If I'm not studying, I'm working.  (if it's not one thing it's the other)	Wǒ búshì niànshū jiùshi gōngzuò.	我不是念书就是工作。
So long as you're willing to take me out for a meal, I'll help you.	Zhǐyào nǐ kěn qǐng wǒ chīfàn jiù bāng nǐ de máng.	只要你肯请我吃饭我就帮你的忙。
So long as you have money, you can buy what you like.	Zhǐyào yǒu qián jiù kěyǐ mǎi nǐ xǐhuan de dōngxī.	只要有钱就可以买你喜欢的东西。
As long as a house is comfortable, what difference does it make if it's beautiful.	Fángzi zhǐyào zhùde shūfu, piàoliang bú piàoliang yòu yǒu shénme guānxī ne?	房子只要住得舒服，漂亮不漂亮又有什么关系呢？
So long as a friend is good natured, what's the difference if he's rich or not?	Péngyǒu zhǐyào xìngqíng hǎo, yǒu qián méiyǒu qián yòu yǒu shénme guānxī ne?	朋友只要性情好，有钱没有钱又有什么关系呢？
This book is just three dollars.  How cheap!	Zhè běn shū cái sān kuài qián, zhēn piányi.	这本书才三块钱，真便宜。
The teacher uses exams as a way to force students to study.	Lǎoshī yòng kǎoshì de fǎzi lái bī xuéshēng niànshū.	老师用考试的法子来逼学生念书。
I know a website that teaches Chinese.	Wǒ zhīdào yíge jiāo zhōngwén de wǎngzhàn.	我知道一个教中文的网站。
He passed away.	Tā qùshì le.	他去世了。
She's a very capable young widow.	Tā shì ge hěn nénggàn de niánqīng guǎfù.	她是个很能干的年轻寡妇。
She expected a lot of him.  (had rigorous demands)	Tā duì tā de yāoqiú hěn yán.	她对他的要求很严。
She made him get up early in the morning to study.	Tā qīngzǎo jiù jiào tā qǐlái dúshū.	她清早就叫他起来读书。
She never reproached him	Tā cónglái bù zébèi tā.	她从来不责备他。
If he made a mistake she punished him (corporally).	Fànle cuò, jiù tǐfá tā.	犯了错就体罚他。
After he got famous, he was grateful for the education she gave him.	Chéngmíng yǐhòu, gǎnjī tā gěi tā de jiàoyù.	成名以后感激她给他的教育。
This is his greatest contribution to China.	Zhè shi tā duì zhōngguó zuì dà de gòngxiàn.	这是他对中国最大的贡献。
He promotes vernacular language.  (i.e. not writing in classical Chinese)	Tā tíchàng báihuàwén.	他提倡白话文。
Previously, Chinese people wrote in classical Chinese.	Cóngqián zhōngguórén dōu xiě wényánwén.	从前中国人都写文言文。
He proposed that we write as we speak.	Tā zhǔzhāng zěnme shuō jiù zěnme xiě.	他主张怎么说就怎么写。
Written language should reflect spoken language.	Xiěde wénzì yīnggāi fǎnyìng shuōde yǔyán.	写的文字应该反映说的语言。
The men of each period should write that period's literary works.	Shénme shídài de rén yīnggāi xiě shénme shídài de wénzhāng.	什么时代的人应该写什么时代的文章。
These ideas are already accepted by everyone.	Zhè xiē yìjiàn xiànzài yǐjīng bèi dàjiā jiēshòule.	这些意见现在已经被大家接受了。
They believed vernacular language was only for people without learning.	Tāmen rènwéi báihuàwén shi méiyǒu xuéwèn de rén cái yòngde.	他们认为白话文是没有学问的人才用的。
He studied abroad in China for seven years.	Tā zài zhōngguó liúxué qī nián.	他在中国留学七年。
They needed democracy, not to revive old systems.	Tāmen xūyàode shi mínzhǔ, ér búshì huīfù jiù zhìdù.	他们需要的是民主而不是恢复旧制度。
He frequently points out unreasonable (societal) phenomena.	Tā shícháng zhǐchū bù hélǐ de xiànxiàng.	他时常指出不合理的现象。
Filial piety and widow's chastity are both fundamental concepts of Chinese culture.	Xiàoshùn, shǒujié dōu shi zhōngguó wénhuà zhōng de jīběn gàiniàn.	孝顺，守节都是中国文化中的基本概念。
Regarding the unequal treatment of women he had profound criticisms.	Duì fùnǚ shòudào de bù píngděng dàiyù tā yǒu shēnkè de pīpàn.	对妇女受到不平等待遇他有深刻的批判。
This is worthwhile for us to study.	Zhè shi zhídé wǒmen xuéxíde.	这是值得我们学习的。
Hu Shi promoted individualism and women's liberation.	Húshì tíchàng gèrénzhǔyì hé fùnǚ jiěfàng.	胡适提倡个人主义和妇女解放。
Due to his all along persistently advocating democratic freedom...	Yóuyú tā shǐzhōng jiānchí mínzhǔ zìyóu de zhǔzhāng...	由于他始终坚持民主自由的主张...
He lived for an extended period in the US.	Tā chángqī zhù zài měiguó.	他长期住在美国。
His ideology served the bourgeoise.  (lit. capitalist class)	Tāde sīxiǎng shi wèi zīchǎnjiējí fúwùde.	他的思想是为资产阶级服务的。
They said he was an imperialist running dog.	Tāmen shuō tā shi dìguózhǔyì de pǎogǒu.	他们说他是帝国主义的跑狗。
He is a Chinese traitor to the Chinese people.	Tā shi chūmài zhōngguó rénmín de hànjiān.	他是出卖中国人民的汉奸。
This kind of critique is just political propaganda.	Zhè zhǒng pīpíng zhǐ shì zhèngzhì xuānchuán.	这种批评只是政治宣传。
He made enormous contributions toward China's modernization.	Tā wèi zhōngguó de xiàndàihuà zuòchūle jùdà de gòngxiàn.	他为中国的现代化做出了巨大的贡献。

He's not a student, but rather a professor.	Tā búshì xuéshēng érshi jiàoshòu.	他不是学生而是教授。
Please turn off the light.	Qǐng guān dēng.	请关灯。

While you're at it, could you check for me to see if there are any other problems?	Nǐ shùnbiàn bāng wǒ jiǎnchá yíxià hái yǒu méiyǒu qítā wèntí.	你顺便帮我检查一下还有没有其他问题。
It's not like you were forced (to do it that way).	Hái búshì bèi bīde.	还不是被逼的。
You yourself wanted to do it this way, no one forced you.	Shì nǐ zìjǐ yuànyì zhème zuòde, méi rén bī nǐ.	是你自己愿意这么做的，没人逼你。
She always makes me drink milk.	Tā zǒng shi bī wǒ hē niúnǎi.	她总是逼我喝牛奶。
Deng Xiaoping: We lived through the Cultural Revolution.	Dèng Xiǎopíng: Wǒmen jīnglì le wénhuà dàgémìng.	邓小平：我们经历了“文化大革命”。
What did you get on the test?  I got a 90.	Nǐ kǎole jǐ fēn?  Jiǔshí fēn.	你考了几分？九十分。
He's a youth, he's still young.	Tā shi ge qīngnián. Tā hái niánqīng.	他是个青年。他还年轻。
Some people wish to be forever young.	Yǒu rén xīwàng zìjǐ yǒngyuǎn niánqīng.	有人希望自己永远年轻。
He's taking this match very seriously.	Tā fēicháng zhòngshì zhè cì bǐsài.	他非常重视这次比赛。

It makes him feel frustrated.  (at being treated unfairly)	Shǐ tā juéde hěn wěiqū.	使他觉得很委屈。
They're worried his girlfriend will get pregnant.	Tāmen dānxīn tā nǚpéngyǒu huáiyùn.	他们担心他女朋友怀孕。
At that time, the child will become a big problem.	Dàoshíhòu háizi huì chéngwéi dà wèntí.	到时候孩子会成为大问题。
Actually, contraception methods are now very advanced.	Qíshí xiànzài bìyùn de fāngfǎ jìnbù de hěn.	其实现在避孕的方法进步得很。
Moreover, even if you get pregnant, abortion is legal.	Zàishuō jiùshi huáileyùn, duòtāi yě shi héfǎ de.	再说就是怀了孕，堕胎也是合法的。
This operation is even easier than pulling a tooth.	Zhège shǒushù bǐ bá yì kē yá hái róngyì.	这个手术比拔一颗牙还容易。
I'm not going to meddle.	Wǒ bù zhǔzhāng gānshè.	我不主张干涉。
The problem is how to live, to support his girlfriend.	Wèntí shi zěnme wéichí shēnghuó, fùdān tā de nǚpéngyǒu.	问题是怎么维持生活，负担他的女朋友。
In my last letter I mentioned the thing about the camera getting stolen.	Shàngcì xìnlǐ, tídào tōu zhàoxiàngjī de shì.	上次信里，提到偷照相机的事。
Now the case is cleared up, turns out it was a student who stole it.	Xiànzài pòàn le, yuánlái shi ge xuéshēng tōude.	现在破案了，原来是个学生偷的。
Reportedly, he has a drug habit.	Jùshuō tā yǒu xīdú de xíguàn.	据说他有吸毒的习惯。
When the drug addiction (craving) hits, he often steals things to buy drugs.	Dúyǐn fā de shíhòu tā cháng tōu dōngxi lái mǎi dúpǐn.	毒瘾发的时候他常偷东西来买毒品。
This reminds me of how it was when I was little.	Zhè shǐ wǒ xiǎngqi wǒ xiǎo shíhòu de qíngxíng.	这使我想起我小时候的情形。
Hearing this bad news makes people very sad.	Tīngdào zhège huài xiāoxi shǐ rén hěn nánguò.	听到这个坏消息使人很难过。
Moreover, it's also close to where you work.	Zàishuō lí nǐ shàngbānde dìfang yòu jìn.	再说离你上班的地方又近。
Even if you graduate college, you won't necessarily be able to find a job.	Jiùshi dàxué bìyè yě bù yídìng zhǎodedào gōngzuò.	就是大学毕业也不一定找得到工作。
Even if you're against this, I'm still going to do it.	Jiùshi nǐ fǎnduì zhè jiàn shì wǒ yě yào zuò.	就是你反对这件事我也要做。
Even a little kid can read this word. (two ways)	(Lián/Jiùshi) xiǎo háir yě kàndedǒng zhè ge zì.	(连/就是)小孩儿也看得懂这个字。
Walking is even faster than driving.	Zǒulù bǐ kāichē hái kuài.	走路比开车还快。
No matter whether you sell it or give it away, no one will mind.	Nǐ mài yěhǎo, sòng rén yěhǎo, méiyǒu rén huì guǎn nǐ. 	你卖也好，送人也好，没有人会管你。
Be it students or teachers, no one likes exams.	Xuéshēng yěhǎo, lǎoshī yěhǎo, dōu bù xǐhuān kǎoshì.	学生也好，老是也好，都不喜欢考试。
Whether it's the city or the country, there are people everywhere.  (i.e. it's crowded with them)	Chénglǐ yěhǎo, xiāngxià yěhǎo, dàochù dōu shi rén.	城里也好，乡下也好，到处都是人。
I was shocked.  (i.e had no idea)	Wǒ dàchīyìjīng.	我大吃一惊。
I sure didn't think your attitude toward pregnancy was so casual.	Wǒ méi xiǎngdào nǐ duì huáiyùn de kànfǎ jìng shi zhème suíbiàn.	我没想到你对怀孕的看法竟是这么随便。
The fetus in the mother's body is a living thing.	Mǔtǐli de tāi shi yíge shēngmìng.	母体里的胎是一个生命。
Any person has the right to go on living.	Rènhé rén dōu yǒu huóxiaqu de quánlì.	任何人都有活下去的权利。
Even a fetus shouldn't be excepted.  (i.e. from this protection)	Jiùshi tāi yě bù yīnggāi lìwài.	就是胎也不应该例外。
To put it another way, ...	Huàn yíjù huà shuō, ...	换一句话说...
Just because the fetus is still small, we can't thoughtlessly murder it.	Wǒmen bù néng yīnwèi tāi hái xiǎo jiù suíyì shāhài.	我们不能因为胎还小就随意杀害。
Good thing you reminded me.	Hái hǎo nǐ tíxǐng wǒ.	还好你提醒我。
I'm simply thinking to give you a little reminder.	Wǒ wúfēi shi xiǎng tíxǐng nǐ yíxià.	我无非是想提醒你一下。
The only thing they know in life is looking for excitement.	Tāmen zhǐ zhīdào zài shēnghuó zhōng zhǎo cìjī.	他们只知道在生活中找刺激。
They think sex is love.	Tāmen yǐwéi zuòài jiùshi àiqíng.	他们以为做爱就是爱情。
These ideas perhaps still have some points worth considering.	Zhè xiē yìjiàn huòxǔ yě hái yǒu yì xiē zhídé cānkǎo de dìfang.	这些意见或许也还有一些值得参考的地方。
I'd advise you not to wait.	Wǒ quàn nǐ bié děng le.	我劝你别等了。
Don't tell me what to do. (i.e. I don't need advice)	Nǐ bié quàn wǒ le.	你别劝我了。
Regarding your boyfriend, I also have a bit of an objection.	Guānyú nǐ de nánpéngyǒu wǒ yě yǒu diǎnr yìjiàn.	关于你的男朋友我也有点儿意见。
His learning and character are both good.	Tā de xuéshì, rénpǐn dōu hěn hǎo.	他的学识，人品都很好。
This inevitably makes me worry a bit about your future.	Zhè miǎnbùliǎo ràng wǒ duì nǐ de jiānglái yǒu xiē dānxīn.	这免不了让我对你的将来有些担心。
Your skin colors are different.	Nǐmen de fūsè bùtóng.	你们的肤色不同。
Your cultural backgrounds are very different.	Nǐmen wénhuà de bèijǐng yǒu hěn dà de chāyì.	你们文化的背景有很大的差异。
Your children will be discriminated against.	Nǐmen de háizi huì shòudào qíshì.	你们的孩子会受到歧视。
I hope you'll be able to think these questions over.	Wǒ xīwàng nǐ néng kǎolǜ yíxià zhè xiē wèntí.	我希望你能考虑一下这些问题。
Lu Xun is an influential critic.	Lǔ Xùn shi yǒu yǐngxiǎnglì de pīpíngjiā.	鲁迅是有影响力的批评家。
He was born into a prosperous Zhejiang family.	Tā chūshēng zài zhèjiāng yíge fùyù de jiātíngli.	他出生在浙江一个富裕的家庭里。
The family's economic situation suddenly deteriorated.  (lit. became impoverished)	Jiātíng de jīngjì qíngkuàng tūrán biànde hěn qióngkùn.	家庭的经济情况突然变的很穷困。
This kind of experience gave him first-hand acquaintance with a different kind of life.	Zhè zhǒng jīnglì ràng tā tǐyàn le bùtóng de shēnghuó.	这种经历让他体验了不同的生活。
His childhood memories became the best material for his writings.	Tā tóngnián de huíyì chéngle tā xiězuò zuì hǎo de cáiliào.	他童年的回忆成了他写作最好的材料。
He thought Chinese medicine practitioners were no more than intentional or unintentional swindlers.	Tā rènwéi zhōngyī búguò shi yǒuyì huò wúyì de piànzi.	他认为中医不过是有意或无意的骗子。
He planned to study western medicine to treat Chinese people.	Tā dǎsuàn xué xīyī lái zhì zhōngguórén de bìng.	他打算学西医来治中国人的病。
A chance occasion made him realize that the problem was spiritual.  (i.e. not physical illness)	Tā zài yícì ǒurán de jīhuìlǐ rènshidào wèntí shi zài jīngshén.	他在一次偶然的机会里认识到问题是在精神。
A pack of fools can be eradicated even if they're healthy.	Yìqún yúmèi de rén jiùshi shēntǐ jiànkāng háishi huì bèi xiāomiè de.	一群愚昧的人就是身体健康还是会被消灭的。
He pursued a career in the arts.	Tā cóngshì wényì gōngzuò.	他从事文艺工作。
He used literary works to awaken the Chinese.	Tā yòngle wénxué zuòpǐn lái huànxǐng zhōngguórén.	他用了文学作品来唤醒中国人。
He composed the short story Diary of a Madman.	Tā chuàngzuòle duǎnpiān xiǎoshuō: kuángrénrìjì.	他创作了短篇小说：狂人日记。
These famous works were all published around the time of the May 4 Movement.	Zhè xiē zhùmíng de zuòpǐn dōu shi zài wǔsìyùndòng qiánhòu fābiǎode.	这些著名的作品都是在五四运动前后发表的。
The purpose of novels was generally entertainment.	Xiǎoshuō de zuòyòng wǎngwǎng shi wèile yúlè.	小说的作用往往是为了娱乐。
Few intellectuals seriously pursued the production of novels.	Zhīshìfènzǐ hěn shǎo rènzhēnde cóngshì xiǎoshuō chuàngzuò.	知识分子很少认真地从事小说创作。
He intentionally used literary works to improve society.	Tā yǒuyì de yòng wénxué zuòpǐn lái gǎiliáng shèhuì.	他有意地用文学作品来改良社会。
He had a serious attitude toward writing.  (didactic rather than for entertainment)	Tā yǒu yánsù de xiězuò tàidu.	他有严肃的写作态度。
His protagonists are generally nobodies neglected by society.	Tā de zhǔjué wǎngwǎng shi búshòu shèhuì zhòngshì de xiǎo rénwù.	他的主角往往是不受社会重视的小人物。
She unexpectedly married someone else.	Tā jìngrán gēn bié rén jiéhūnle.	她竟然跟别人结婚了。
You dare to sell my car!  You're awful.	Nǐ jìng gǎn bǎ wǒde chē màile, nǐ zhēn kě è!	你竟敢把我的车卖了。你真可恶！
I saw the 'tian' character as the character 'da'.	Wǒ bǎ 'tiān' zì kànchéng 'dà' zì le.	我把 '天' 字看成 '大' 字了。
He took his own experiences wrote a book from them.	Tā bǎ zìjǐ de jīngyàn xiěchéng yì běn shū.	他把自己的经验写成一本书。
The students saw the test as a terrifying thing.	Xuéshēng bǎ kǎoshì kànchéng hěn kěpà de shì.	学生把考试看成很可怕的事。
From the point of view of someone who has studied economics...	Zài xuéguo jīngjì de rén kànlái...	在学过经济的人看来...
Every person hopes to live a better life.	Rènhé rén dōu xīwàng shēnghuó guò de hǎo yìdiǎnr.	任何人都希望生活过的好一点儿。
Nobody could forsee that he would become such a famous person.	Rènhé rén dōu kànbuchulai tā huì biànchéng yíge zhème yǒumíng de rén.	任何人都看不出来他会变成这么有名的人。
Regarding this matter, our two views are not the same. (i.e. yours and mine)	Guānyú zhè jiàn shì, wǒmen liǎngge rén de kànfǎ bùtóng.	关于这件事，我们两个人的看法不同。
He likes to discuss political questions.	Tā xǐhuān tán guānyú zhèngzhì de wèntí.	他喜欢谈关于政治的问题。
The books he bought are about Chinese history.	Tā mǎide shū shi guānyú zhōngguó lìshǐ de.	他买的书是关于中国历史的。
The movie I saw yesterday was about American society.	Wǒ zuótiān kànde diànyǐng shi guānyú měiguó shèhuì de.	我昨天看的电影是关于美国社会的。
The paper is about Sino-Japanese economic relations.	Bàogào shi guānyú rìběn hé zhōngguó de jīngjì guānxì de.	报告是关于日本和中国的经济关系的。
Marrying someone with such a weird nature, you can't avoid divorce.	Nǐ gēn xìngqíng zhème qíguài de rén jiéhūn, miǎnbuliǎo líhūn.	你跟性情这么奇怪的人结婚，免不了离婚。
Arguments are inevitable.	Chǎojià shi miǎnbuliǎo de.	吵架是免不了的。
Driving fast inevitably leads to accidents.	Kāi kuài chē miǎnbuliǎo huì chūshì.	开快车免不了会出事。
The protagonist is an impoverished peasant.	Zhǔjué shi yíge pínkùn de nóngrén.	主角是一个贫困的农人。
He's a frustrated intellectual.  (i.e. disappointed in his ambitions)	Tā shi yíge shīyì de zhīshìfènzǐ.	他是一个失意的知识分子。
These stories reflected Chinese society at the end of the Qing dynasty and beginning of the ROC.	Zhè xiē gùshi fǎnyìngle qīngmò mínchū zhōngguó de shèhuì.	这些故事反映了清末民初中国的社会。
They also without at all holding back exposed the cruelty of the Chinese.	Yě háobù bǎoliúde jiēlùle zhōngguórén de cánkù.	也毫不保留地揭露了中国人的残酷。
His stories exposed the hypocrisy of the Chinese.	Tāde gùshi jiēlùle zhōngguórén de xūjiǎ.	他的故事揭露了中国人的虚假。
He unreservedly discussed the ignorance and selfishness of the Chinese.	Tā bù bǎoliúde tánle zhōngguórén de yúmèi hé zìsī.	他不保留地谈了中国人的愚昧和自私。
After he was middle-aged, Lu Xun wrote a great many essays. (i.e. his signature type)	Lǔxùn zhōngnián yǐhòu xiěle dàliàng de záwén.	鲁迅中年以后写了大量的杂文。
willing to talk about anything, omniscient, omnipotent	wúsuǒbùtán, wúsuǒbùzhī, wúsuǒbùnéng	无所不谈，无所不知，无所不能
From history to current trends he expressed his opinions.	Cóng lìshǐ dào shíshì tā dōu biǎoshìle tā de yìjiàn.	从历史到时事他都表示了他的意见。
The characteristic thing of his essays was the satiric overtone.	Tā záwén de tèdiǎn shi dàizhe fěngcì de yìwèi.	他杂文的特点是带着讽刺的意味。
Throughout his life he represented the intellectual's multifacted concern for national affairs and current politics.	Tā yìshēng daìbiǎo zhīshìfènzǐ duì guóshì hé shíjú duōfāngmiàn de guānhuái.	他一生代表知识分子对国事和时局多方面的关怀。
He represented the Chinese intellectual's sympathy for the broad swath of common people.	Tā dàibiǎo zhōngguó zhīshìfènzǐ duì guǎngdà lǎobǎixìng de tóngqíng.	他代表中国知识分子对广大老百姓的同情。
This is what he is most worth our remembering for.	Zhè shi tā zuì zhídé wǒmen jìniàn de dìfang.	这是他最值得我们纪念的地方。

Around New Year's plane tickets are especially hard to buy.	Xīnnián qiánhòu de fēijīpiào tèbié nán mǎi.	新年前后的飞机票特别难买。
Around the time of the Cultural Revolution China, in every respect, was very unstable.	Wénhuàdàgémìng fāshēng qiánhòu zhōngguó wúlùn zài gè fāngmiàn dōu hěn bù āndìng.	文化大革命发生前后中国无论在各方面都很不安定。
He's a writer. (two ways)	Tā shi zuòjiā/zuòzhě.	他是作家/作者。
We better memorize as many sentence patterns as we can.	Wǒmen zuì hǎo jǐn kěnéng duō bèi jùxíng.	我们最好尽可能多背句型。
When it's time to go on vacation, if students don't go home, they travel.  (if not one, then the other)	Fàngjià de shíhòu xuéshēng búshì huíjiā jiùshi qù lǚxíng.	放假的时候学生不是回家就是去旅行。
Tomorrow is a day off.	Míngtiān yào fàngjiàle.	明天要放假了。
This is not considered important by the government.	Zhè bú shòu zhèngfǔ zhòngshì.	这不受政府重视。
There's a generation gap between us.	Wǒmen zhījiān yǒu yíge dàigōu.	我们之间有一个代沟。
She never thought that her husband would leave her.	Tā cónglái méiyǒu xiǎngdào tā de zhàngfu huì líkāi tā.	她从来没有想到她的丈夫会离开她。
Over the past year and more, we've been together a lot.  (e.g. romantically)	Guòqù yìnián duō lái, wǒmen jiāowǎng bǐjiào duō.	过去一年多来，我们交往比较多。
He's sincere with people.	Tā dàirén chéngkěn.	他待人诚恳。
He's filled with confidence about the future.	Tā duì jiānglái chōngmǎn xìnxīn.	他对将来充满信心。
He goes on and on about the same stuff.	Tā shuōláishuōqù zǒng shi lǎoyītào.	他说来说去总是老一套。
Interracial marriage is a common thing.	Bùtóng rénzhǒng jiéhūn shi yíjiàn píngcháng de shì.	不同人种结婚是一件平常的事。
I'd like to work for a few years.	Wǒ xiǎng zuò jǐ nián shì.	我想做几年事。
He's had professional success.	Tā zài shìyè yǒule chéngjì.	他在事业有了成绩。
The idea that women should take care of housework is out of date.	Nǚrén yīnggāi guǎn jiāshì de guānniàn jiù guòshí le.	女人应该管家事的观念就过时了。
I sometimes feel indignant regarding mom.	Wǒ yǒushí jiù wèi mǔqīn bàobùpíng.	我有时就为母亲抱不平。
Her whole life's work is cleaning up the house.	Tā yíbèizi de gōngzuò jiù shi dǎsǎo fángzi.	她一辈子的工作就是打扫房子。
Passing your whole life this way is not only monotonous, but boring as well.	Zhèyàng guò yíbèizi búdàn tài dāndiào yě tài wúliáo le.	这样过一辈子不但太单调也太无聊了。
I can't sacrifice my own career for the sake of the family.	Wǒ shì búhuì wèile jiātíng jiù xīshēng zìjǐ de shìyè de.	我是不会为了家庭就牺牲自己的事业的。
For the time being, he won't talk about getting married.	Zànshí bùtán jiéhūn.	暂时不谈结婚。
He has no confidence in himself at all.	Tā duì zìjǐ yìdiǎnr yě méiyǒu xìnxīn.	他对自己一点儿也没有信心。
I've looked at this over and over...still can't make out whose writing it is.	Wǒ kànláikànqù dōu kànbuchulai zhè shi shéi xiěde zì.	我看来看去都看不出来这是谁写的字。
After he said it over and over, I finally understood.	Tā shuōláishuōqù, wǒ zhōngyú tīngdǒngle.	他说来说去，我终于听懂了。
I have misgivings about this issue.	Wǒ duì zhè ge wèntí gùlù.	我对这个问题顾虑。
He sacrificed his life for the country.	Tā wèi guójiā xīshēngle shēngmìng.	他为国家牺牲了生命。
I'm really concerned about your illness.	Wǒ zhēn wèi nǐ de bìng dānxīn.	我真为你的病担心。
Wash the vegetables first and wait till after the guests arrive to cut them.	Nǐ xiān xǐ cài, děng kèrén láile yǐhòu zài qiē.	你先洗菜，等客人来了以后再切。
In terms of studying, he's very diligent.	Zài xuéxíshàng, tā hěn nǔlì.	在学习上，他很努力。
What was the state of the family like?	Jiātíng zhuàngkuàng rúhé?	家庭状况如何？
Everyone says she's pretty, but in fact she's ugly.	Dàjiā shuō tā hěn piàoliang, shìshíshàng tā hěn chǒu.	大家说她很漂亮，事实上她很丑。
This is a fact.	Zhè jiùshi shìshí.	这就是事实。
He always likes to exaggerate the facts.	Tā zǒng shi xǐhuān kuādà shìshí.	他总是喜欢夸大事实。
He looks honest, but in fact he loves to lie.	Tā kànqǐlai hěn lǎoshi, shìshíshàng hěn ài shuōhuǎng.	他看起来很老实，事实上很爱说谎。
This movie is absolutely fantastic.	Zhè ge diànyǐng shífēn jīngcǎi.	这个电影十分精彩。
He's full of prejudice.	Tā chōngmǎn chéngjiàn.	他充满成见。
It expresses the author's biases and childishness.	Biǎoshì zuòzhě de piānjiàn gēn yòuzhì.	表示作者的偏见跟幼稚。
It everywhere expresses the author's female-disrespecting male chauvinism.	Chùchù biǎoshì zuòzhě bù zūnzhòng nǚxìng de dànánrénzhǔyì.	处处表示作者不尊重女性的大男人主义。
He uses pornographic and violent topics to attract our interest.	Tā yòng sèqíng gēn bàolì de tímù lái yǐnqǐ wǒmen de xìngqu.	他用色情跟暴力的题目来引起我们的兴趣。
Teaching a language isn't at all a matter of promoting a product.	Jiāo yǔyán bìng búshì tuīxiāo chǎnpǐn.	较语言并不是推销产品。
There's no need to use TV advertising methods to excite students.	Yòngbuzháo ná diànshì guǎnggào de bànfǎ lái cìjī xuéshēng.	用不着拿电视广告的办法来刺激学生。
I don't like this kind of teaching material.	Wǒ bù xǐhuān zhè yàng de jiàocái.	我不喜欢这样的教材。
A says...B says...	Jiǎ shuō...yǐ shuō...	甲说...乙说...
You're really a hypocrite.	Nǐ zhēn shi yíge wěijūnzǐ.	你真是一个伪君子。
Why can't these topics be taken and used as language teaching material?	Wèishénme zhè xiē tímù bùnéng nálái zuò yǔyán jiàocái ne?	为什么这些题目不能拿来做语言教材呢？
Some of his ideas are perhaps a little extreme.	Tā yǒu xiē yìjiàn yěxǔ shi tài jíduānle yìdiǎnr.	他有些意见也许太极端了一点儿。
If every story just teaches us to be good people, that's just boring.	Rúguǒ měige gùshi dōu zhǐ shi jiāo wǒmen zuò hǎo rén, nà cái wúliáo ne.	如果每个故事只是较我们做好人，那才无聊呢。
As for abortion being even easier than pulling a tooth...	Zhìyú duòtāi bǐ báyá hái róngyì... 	至于堕胎比拔牙还容易...
He just wants to explain that modern medicine is very advanced.	Tā zhǐ shi xiǎng shuōmíng xiàndài yīxué hěn jìnbù.	他只是想说明现代医学很进步。
It has nothing to do with discriminating against women.	Gēn qíshì nǚrén shi méiyǒu guānxi de.	跟歧视女人是没有关系的。
The author doesn't necessarily have this idea in mind.	Zuòzhě bújiàndé yǒu zhège yìsi.	作者不见得有这个意思。
My language ability is restricted.	Wǒde yǔyán nénglì hěn xiànzhì.	我的语言能力很限制。
It can't help having the defect of being superficial.	Miǎnbuliǎo yǒu fūqiǎn de máobìng.	免不了有肤浅的毛病。
It can't help having the defect of being childish.	Miǎnbuliǎo yǒu yòuzhì de máobìng.	免不了有幼稚的毛病。
I don't expect to find the solution to marriage problems.	Wǒ bù xiǎng zhǎodào duì hūnyīn wèntí de dá'àn.	我不想找到对婚姻问题的答案。
What are your thoughts? (e.g. about the movie)	Nǐ yǒu shénme gǎnxiǎng?	你有什么感想？
Blogs are for writing thoughts.	Bókè shi xiě sīxiǎngde.	博客是写思想的。
Flying in a plane is both safe and comfortable.	Zuò feījī jì ānquán yòu shūfu.	坐飞机既安全又舒服。
The movie is filled with violence.	Diànyǐnglǐ chōngmǎn le bàolì.	电影里充满了暴力。
Children cry to get adults' attention.	Xiǎoháir kū shi yīnwèi yǐnqǐ dàrén de zhùyì.	小孩儿哭是因为引起大人的注意。
That puppy got everyone's sympathy.	Nà zhī xiǎogǒu yǐnqǐ le dàjiā de tóngqíng.	那只小狗引起了大家的同情。
You don't have to be angry; he's already apologized to you.	Nǐ yòngbuzháo shēngqì, tā yǐjīng gēn nǐ dàoqiànle.	你用不着生气，他已经跟你道歉了。
My illness isn't serious; there's no need to see a doctor.	Wǒde bìng bù yánzhòng, yòngbuzháo kàn dàifu.	我的病不严重，用不着看大夫。
If it's useful, buy it.	Yàoshi yòngdezháo jiù mǎi ba.	要是用得着就买吧。
He's always lying, I'll never believe him again.	Tā zǒngshi piànrén, wǒ zàiyě búhuì xiāngxìn tā le.	他总是骗人，我再也不会相信他了。
I'll never come again.	Wǒ zàiyě bùlái le.	我再也不来了。
He never came back again.	Tā zàiyě méi huíláiguo.	他再也没回来过。
Don't buy this kind of candy again.	Zàiyě bié mǎi zhè zhǒng táng le.	再也别买这种糖了。
It integrates experience and knowledge.	Bǎ jīngyàn gēn zhīshì jiéhéqilái.	把经验跟知识结合起来。
